--- filename: \src\components\bottles\BottleRow.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useTransition } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import {
  setBottleStatusAction,
  consumeBottleQuantityAction,
} from "@/lib/actions/bottles";
import { Card } from "@/components/ui/Card";
import { formatDate } from "@/lib/date";
import type { BottleWithCustomer } from "@/lib/data/bottles";
import type { BottleStatus } from "@/types/database";

const STATUS_OPTIONS: { value: BottleStatus; label: string }[] = [
  { value: "kept",     label: "鬆舌°繧贋ｸｭ" },
  { value: "finished", label: "鬟ｲ縺ｿ蛻・ｊ" },
  { value: "returned", label: "霑泌唆" },
  { value: "disposed", label: "蟒・｣・ },
];

const STATUS_LABEL: Record<string, string> = {
  kept:     "差 鬆舌°繧贋ｸｭ",
  finished: "鬟ｲ縺ｿ蛻・ｊ貂・,
  returned: "霑泌唆貂・,
  disposed: "蟒・｣・ｸ・,
};

export function BottleRow({ bottle }: { bottle: BottleWithCustomer }) {
  const [editing, setEditing] = useState(false);
  const [partialConsumeOpen, setPartialConsumeOpen] = useState(false);
  const [consumeQuantity, setConsumeQuantity] = useState(1);
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();

  return (
    <Card className="flex flex-col gap-3">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 flex-wrap">
        <div className="min-w-0">
          <Link
            href={`/customers/${bottle.customer_id}`}
            className="font-bold text-navy text-base hover:underline"
          >
            {bottle.customer_display_name}
          </Link>
          <span className="text-navy/70 ml-2 text-sm">
            {bottle.bottle_type && <span className="font-bold">{bottle.bottle_type}</span>}
            {bottle.bottle_type && bottle.bottle_name && bottle.bottle_name !== bottle.bottle_type && (
              <span className="text-navy/40">・・bottle.bottle_name}・・/span>
            )}
            {!bottle.bottle_type && bottle.bottle_name}
            {bottle.quantity > 1 && <span className="text-navy/40 text-xs ml-1">ﾃ養bottle.quantity}</span>}
          </span>
          <p className="text-xs text-navy/40 mt-0.5">
            逋ｻ骭ｲ・嘴formatDate(bottle.start_date)}縲迥ｶ諷具ｼ嘴STATUS_LABEL[bottle.status] ?? bottle.status}
          </p>
          {bottle.companion_names && bottle.companion_names.length > 0 && (
            <p className="text-xs font-bold text-info mt-1 bg-info/5 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5 inline-block">
              則 蜷御ｼｴ・嘴bottle.companion_names.join("縲・)}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {bottle.status === "kept" && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setEditing((v) => !v)}
              className="btn-base px-4 min-h-11 bg-navy text-white text-sm"
            >
              迥ｶ諷句､画峩
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 迥ｶ諷句､画峩繝代ロ繝ｫ */}
      {editing && (
        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start gap-3 border-t border-navy/10 pt-3">
          {/* 荳驛ｨ豸郁ｲｻ */}
          {bottle.quantity > 1 && bottle.status === "kept" && (
            <div className="w-full flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 bg-warn/5 rounded-app p-3">
              <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold text-navy/60 w-full">
                <input
                  type="checkbox"
                  checked={partialConsumeOpen}
                  onChange={(e) => setPartialConsumeOpen(e.target.checked)}
                  className="w-4 h-4 accent-warn"
                />
                荳驛ｨ縺縺大､画峩縺吶ｋ・・bottle.quantity}譛ｬ荳ｭ・・              </label>
              {partialConsumeOpen && (
                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    min={1}
                    max={bottle.quantity}
                    value={consumeQuantity}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setConsumeQuantity(
                        Math.max(1, Math.min(bottle.quantity, Number(e.target.value) || 1))
                      )
                    }
                    className="w-16 min-h-10 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-2 text-sm text-center"
                  />
                  <span className="text-sm text-navy/50">譛ｬ繧・/span>
                  {(["finished", "returned", "disposed"] as const).map((s) => (
                    <button
                      key={s}
                      type="button"
                      disabled={pending}
                      onClick={() =>
                        startTransition(() => consumeBottleQuantityAction(bottle.id, consumeQuantity, s))
                      }
                      className="btn-base px-3 min-h-10 bg-warn/10 border-2 border-warn/30 text-warn text-sm font-bold disabled:opacity-40"
                    >
                      {STATUS_OPTIONS.find((o) => o.value === s)?.label}縺ｫ
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 蜈ｨ驛ｨ螟画峩 */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {STATUS_OPTIONS.filter((o) => o.value !== bottle.status).map((o) => (
              <button
                key={o.value}
                type="button"
                disabled={pending}
                onClick={() =>
                  startTransition(() => setBottleStatusAction(bottle.id, o.value))
                }
                className="btn-base px-4 min-h-11 bg-white border-2 border-navy/10 text-navy/60 text-sm disabled:opacity-40"
              >
                {bottle.quantity > 1 ? "蜈ｨ驛ｨ " : ""}
                {o.label}縺ｫ螟画峩
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </Card>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\bottles\BottleStatusFilterBar.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useRouter, usePathname, useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import type { BottleStatusFilter } from "@/lib/data/bottles";

// v1.2: 繝懊ヨ繝ｫ譛滄剞蟒・ｭ｢縺ｮ縺溘ａ expiring30/expired 繝輔ぅ繝ｫ繧ｿ繝ｼ繧貞炎髯､
const OPTIONS: { value: BottleStatusFilter; label: string; emoji: string }[] = [
  { value: "kept",     label: "鬆舌°繧贋ｸｭ", emoji: "差" },
  { value: "finished", label: "鬟ｲ縺ｿ蛻・ｊ", emoji: "" },
  { value: "returned", label: "霑泌唆",     emoji: "" },
  { value: "disposed", label: "蟒・｣・,     emoji: "" },
];

export function BottleStatusFilterBar({ selected }: { selected: BottleStatusFilter[] }) {
  const router    = useRouter();
  const pathname  = usePathname();
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();

  function select(value: BottleStatusFilter) {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(searchParams.toString());
    params.delete("status");
    params.delete("page");
    const alreadySelected = selected.length === 1 && selected[0] === value;
    if (!alreadySelected) params.append("status", value);
    router.push(`${pathname}?${params.toString()}`);
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4">
      {OPTIONS.map((opt) => (
        <button
          key={opt.value}
          type="button"
          onClick={() => select(opt.value)}
          className={`px-4 py-2.5 rounded-app text-base font-bold border-2 transition-colors ${
            selected.includes(opt.value)
              ? "bg-navy text-white border-navy"
              : "bg-white text-navy/60 border-navy/10"
          }`}
        >
          {opt.emoji} {opt.label}
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\calendar\CalendarClient.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, History } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/Card";
import { yen } from "@/lib/date";
import type { CalendarMonthData } from "@/lib/data/calendar";

const WEEKDAYS = ["譌･", "譛・, "轣ｫ", "豌ｴ", "譛ｨ", "驥・, "蝨・];

const STATUS_LABEL: Record<string, string> = {
  reserved: "莠育ｴ・ｸｭ",
  visited: "譚･蠎玲ｸ医∩",
};

function calendarLink(year: number, month: number): string {
  return `/calendar?year=${year}&month=${month}`;
}

export function CalendarClient({ data }: { data: CalendarMonthData }) {
  const { year, month, days } = data;
  const today = new Date();
  const todayStr = `${today.getFullYear()}-${String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}-${String(
    today.getDate()
  ).padStart(2, "0")}`;

  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState<string | null>(
    year === today.getFullYear() && month === today.getMonth() + 1 ? todayStr : null
  );

  const firstDay = new Date(year, month - 1, 1);
  const startWeekday = firstDay.getDay();
  const daysInMonth = new Date(year, month, 0).getDate();

  const prevMonthDate = new Date(year, month - 2, 1);
  const nextMonthDate = new Date(year, month, 1);
  const lastYearDate = new Date(year - 1, month - 1, 1);

  const cells: (string | null)[] = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < startWeekday; i++) cells.push(null);
  for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
    cells.push(`${year}-${String(month).padStart(2, "0")}-${String(d).padStart(2, "0")}`);
  }

  const selectedDay = selectedDate ? days[selectedDate] : null;

  return (
    <div>
      {/* 繝翫ン繧ｲ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4 flex-wrap gap-2">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Link
            href={calendarLink(prevMonthDate.getFullYear(), prevMonthDate.getMonth() + 1)}
            className="btn-base px-3 min-h-11 bg-white border-2 border-navy/10 text-navy"
          >
            <ChevronLeft size={20} />
          </Link>
          <h2 className="text-xl font-black text-navy w-36 text-center">
            {year}蟷ｴ{month}譛・          </h2>
          <Link
            href={calendarLink(nextMonthDate.getFullYear(), nextMonthDate.getMonth() + 1)}
            className="btn-base px-3 min-h-11 bg-white border-2 border-navy/10 text-navy"
          >
            <ChevronRight size={20} />
          </Link>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <Link
            href={calendarLink(lastYearDate.getFullYear(), lastYearDate.getMonth() + 1)}
            className="btn-base px-3 min-h-11 bg-white border-2 border-navy/10 text-navy text-sm font-bold gap-1.5"
          >
            <History size={16} />蜴ｻ蟷ｴ
          </Link>
          <Link
            href={calendarLink(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() + 1)}
            className="btn-base px-4 min-h-11 bg-gold text-navy font-bold text-sm"
          >
            莉頑律縺ｸ
          </Link>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 莉頑怦蜷郁ｨ・*/}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mb-4">
        <Card className="text-center py-3">
          <p className="text-xs text-navy/50 font-bold mb-1">莉頑怦蜷郁ｨ亥｣ｲ荳・/p>
          <p className="text-2xl font-black text-navy">{yen(data.monthTotalAmount)}</p>
        </Card>
        <Card className="text-center py-3">
          <p className="text-xs text-navy/50 font-bold mb-1">莉頑怦蜷郁ｨ医メ繝・・</p>
          <p className="text-2xl font-black text-navy">{yen(data.monthTotalTip)}</p>
        </Card>
      </div>

      {/* 繧ｫ繝ｬ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ繧ｰ繝ｪ繝・ラ */}
      <Card className="mb-4 p-3">
        {/* 譖懈律繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-7 mb-1">
          {WEEKDAYS.map((w, i) => (
            <div
              key={w}
              className={`text-center text-xs font-bold py-1 ${
                i === 0 ? "text-danger" : i === 6 ? "text-info" : "text-navy/40"
              }`}
            >
              {w}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* 譌･莉倥げ繝ｪ繝・ラ */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-0.5">
          {cells.map((dateStr, idx) => {
            if (!dateStr) return <div key={`empty-${idx}`} />;
            const [dy, dm, dd] = dateStr.split("-").map(Number);
            const dayOfWeek = new Date(dy, dm - 1, dd).getDay();
            const isSunday   = dayOfWeek === 0;
            const isSaturday = dayOfWeek === 6;
            const isToday    = dateStr === todayStr;
            const isSelected = dateStr === selectedDate;
            const day        = days[dateStr];
            const dayNum     = dd;

            const textColor =
              isSunday || (day?.isHoliday)
                ? "text-danger font-black"
                : isSaturday
                ? "text-info font-black"
                : "text-navy/70";

            const bgClass = isSelected
              ? "border-gold bg-gold/20"
              : isToday
              ? "border-navy bg-white"
              : day?.isClosedDay
              ? "border-danger/20 bg-[#fff0f0]"
              : "border-navy/5 bg-white hover:border-navy/20";

            const hasContent =
              (day?.visits.length ?? 0) > 0 ||
              (day?.reservations.length ?? 0) > 0 ||
              (day?.birthdays.length ?? 0) > 0 ||
              (day?.events.length ?? 0) > 0 ||
              day?.isHoliday ||
              day?.isClosedDay;

            return (
              <button
                key={dateStr}
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setSelectedDate(dateStr === selectedDate ? null : dateStr)}
                className={`text-left rounded-app border-2 p-1.5 min-h-[68px] transition-colors ${bgClass}`}
              >
                <span className={`text-sm ${textColor}${isToday ? " bg-navy/10 rounded-full px-1" : ""}`}>
                  {dayNum}
                </span>
                <div className="mt-0.5 flex flex-col gap-0.5">
                  {day?.isClosedDay && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-danger">圻莨・/span>
                  )}
                  {day?.isHoliday && !day.isClosedDay && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-danger/70">閥逾・/span>
                  )}
                  {day?.events.slice(0, 2).map((ev) => (
                    <span key={ev.id} className="text-[10px] leading-none">{ev.emoji}</span>
                  ))}
                  {(day?.visits.length ?? 0) > 0 && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-success">
                      譚･{day.visits.length}
                    </span>
                  )}
                  {(day?.reservations.length ?? 0) > 0 && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-info">
                      莠・day.reservations.length}
                    </span>
                  )}
                  {(day?.birthdays.length ?? 0) > 0 && (
                    <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#7a4fa3]">獅</span>
                  )}
                  {!hasContent && <span className="text-[10px] text-navy/20">窶・/span>}
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </Card>

      {/* 驕ｸ謚樊律縺ｮ隧ｳ邏ｰ */}
      {selectedDay && (
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
          <Card>
            <CardTitle className="text-lg">
              {selectedDate?.replace(/-/g, "/")} 縺ｮ隧ｳ邏ｰ
            </CardTitle>

            {/* 譚･蠎嶺ｸ隕ｧ */}
            <p className="text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-2">譚･蠎・/p>
            {selectedDay.visits.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-navy/40 text-base mb-3">譚･蠎励・縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・/p>
            )}
            <ul className="flex flex-col gap-2 mb-4">
              {selectedDay.visits.map((v) => (
                <li key={v.id} className="rounded-app bg-navy/3 border border-navy/5 p-3">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
                    <p className="font-black text-navy text-base">
                      {v.hasChampagne && <span className="mr-1">裟</span>}
                      {v.customerName}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-sm font-bold text-navy/60">{yen(v.amount)}</p>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-navy/40 mt-0.5">{v.time}</p>
                  {v.companionNames.length > 0 && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-navy/40 mt-0.5">蜷御ｼｴ・嘴v.companionNames.join("縲・)}</p>
                  )}
                </li>
              ))}
            </ul>

            {/* 莠育ｴ・ｸ隕ｧ */}
            <p className="text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-2">莠育ｴ・/p>
            {selectedDay.reservations.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-navy/40 text-base mb-3">莠育ｴ・・縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・/p>
            )}
            <ul className="flex flex-col gap-2 mb-4">
              {selectedDay.reservations.map((r) => (
                <li key={r.id} className="rounded-app bg-info/5 border border-info/20 p-3">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
                    <p className="font-black text-navy text-base">{r.customerName}</p>
                    <span className="text-xs text-info font-bold">{STATUS_LABEL[r.status] ?? r.status}</span>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-navy/40 mt-0.5">{r.time}</p>
                  {r.companionNames.length > 0 && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-navy/40">蜷御ｼｴ・嘴r.companionNames.join("縲・)}</p>
                  )}
                  {r.memo && <p className="text-xs text-navy/40">繝｡繝｢・嘴r.memo}</p>}
                </li>
              ))}
            </ul>

            {/* 隱慕函譌･ */}
            {selectedDay.birthdays.length > 0 && (
              <>
                <p className="text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-2">隱慕函譌･</p>
                <ul className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 mb-4">
                  {selectedDay.birthdays.map((b) => (
                    <li key={b.id} className="text-base font-bold text-[#7a4fa3]">
                      獅 {b.customerName}
                    </li>
                  ))}
                </ul>
              </>
            )}

            {/* 繧､繝吶Φ繝医・莨第律 */}
            {(selectedDay.isHoliday || selectedDay.isClosedDay || selectedDay.events.length > 0) && (
              <>
                <p className="text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-2">繧､繝吶Φ繝医・莨第律</p>
                <ul className="flex flex-col gap-1.5">
                  {selectedDay.isClosedDay && (
                    <li className="text-base font-bold text-danger">
                      圻 蠎嶺ｼ第律{selectedDay.closedNote ? ` 窶・${selectedDay.closedNote}` : ""}
                    </li>
                  )}
                  {selectedDay.isHoliday && (
                    <li className="text-base font-bold text-danger/80">
                      閥 {selectedDay.holidayName}・育･晄律・・                    </li>
                  )}
                  {selectedDay.events.map((ev) => (
                    <li key={ev.id} className="text-base text-navy">
                      {ev.emoji} {ev.title}
                      {ev.url && (
                        <a href={ev.url} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"
                           className="text-xs text-info underline ml-2">
                          迫 隧ｳ邏ｰ
                        </a>
                      )}
                    </li>
                  ))}
                </ul>
              </>
            )}
          </Card>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\BottleAddForm.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useActionState, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { addBottleAction, type BottleFormState } from "@/lib/actions/bottles";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/Button";
import { BOTTLE_TYPE_CANDIDATES } from "@/lib/bottle-types";

const initialState: BottleFormState = { error: null };

export function BottleAddForm({
  customerId,
  autoOpen = false,
}: {
  customerId: string;
  autoOpen?: boolean;
}) {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(autoOpen);
  const [state, formAction, pending] = useActionState(addBottleAction, initialState);
  const [bottleType, setBottleType] = useState("");
  const formRef = useRef<HTMLFormElement>(null);
  const initialStateRef = useRef(state);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (state !== initialStateRef.current && !state.error) {
      formRef.current?.reset();
      setBottleType("");
      setOpen(false);
    }
  }, [state]);

  if (!open) {
    return (
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => setOpen(true)}
        className="btn-base w-full mt-3 bg-warn text-white"
      >
        繝懊ヨ繝ｫ霑ｽ蜉
      </button>
    );
  }

  return (
    <form ref={formRef} action={formAction} className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-3 border-t border-navy/10 pt-3">
      <input type="hidden" name="customer_id" value={customerId} />
      <input type="hidden" name="bottle_type" value={bottleType} />
      {/* 譛滄剞縺ｯDB繝・ヵ繧ｩ繝ｫ繝亥､・育匳骭ｲ譌･+1蟷ｴ・峨ｒ菴ｿ逕ｨ */}

      <span className="block text-xs font-bold text-navy/50">繝懊ヨ繝ｫ縺ｮ遞ｮ鬘・/span>
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
        {BOTTLE_TYPE_CANDIDATES.map((c) => (
          <button
            key={c}
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setBottleType(c)}
            className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold border ${
              bottleType === c ? "bg-gold border-gold text-navy-dark" : "bg-white border-navy/10 text-navy/50"
            }`}
          >
            {c}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={bottleType}
        onChange={(e) => setBottleType(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="蛟呵｣懊↓縺ｪ縺・ｴ蜷医・謇句・蜉・
        className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
      />
      <input
        type="text"
        name="bottle_name"
        placeholder="繝懊ヨ繝ｫ繝阪・繝・医く繝ｼ繝玲惆縺ｫ譖ｸ縺丞錐蜑阪・莉ｻ諢擾ｼ・
        className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
      />
      <label className="block">
        <span className="block text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-1">譛ｬ謨ｰ</span>
        <input
          type="number"
          name="quantity"
          min={1}
          defaultValue={1}
          className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
        />
      </label>
      <input
        type="text"
        name="memo"
        placeholder="繝｡繝｢・井ｻｻ諢擾ｼ・
        className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
      />

      {state.error && <p className="text-danger text-xs font-bold">{state.error}</p>}
      <div className="flex gap-2">
        <Button type="submit" variant="gold" fullWidth disabled={pending}>
          {pending ? "霑ｽ蜉荳ｭ窶ｦ" : "霑ｽ蜉"}
        </Button>
        <Button type="button" variant="outline" onClick={() => setOpen(false)}>
          髢峨§繧・        </Button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\BottleStatusBadge.tsx ---

import type { Bottle } from "@/types/database";
import { getExpiryTier, EXPIRY_TIER_META } from "@/lib/bottle-expiry";

const STATUS_LABEL: Record<Bottle["status"], string> = {
  kept: "鬆舌°繧贋ｸｭ",
  finished: "鬟ｲ縺ｿ蛻・ｊ",
  returned: "霑泌唆",
  disposed: "蟒・｣・,
};

/**
 * 繝懊ヨ繝ｫ縺ｮ迥ｶ諷九ヰ繝・ず縲・ * 鬆舌°繧贋ｸｭ縺ｮ繝懊ヨ繝ｫ縺ｯ譛滄剞縺ｾ縺ｧ縺ｮ譌･謨ｰ縺ｧ5谿ｵ髫弱↓濶ｲ蛻・￠縺吶ｋ・医＃謖・ｮ壻ｻ墓ｧ假ｼ峨・ * 泙31譌･莉･荳・/ 泛30譌･莉･蜀・/ 泯14譌･莉･蜀・/ 閥7譌･莉･蜀・/ 笞ｫ譛滄剞蛻・ｌ
 */
export function BottleStatusBadge({ bottle }: { bottle: Bottle }) {
  if (bottle.status !== "kept") {
    return (
      <span className="text-xs font-bold text-navy/40 bg-navy/5 rounded-full px-2.5 py-1">
        {STATUS_LABEL[bottle.status]}
      </span>
    );
  }

  const tier = getExpiryTier(bottle.expiry_date);
  const { emoji, label, className } = EXPIRY_TIER_META[tier];

  return (
    <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-bold rounded-full px-2.5 py-1 ${className}`}>
      <span aria-hidden>{emoji}</span>
      {label}
    </span>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\CautionToggle.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useTransition } from "react";
import { AlertTriangle, Ban } from "lucide-react";
import { setCautionAction } from "@/lib/actions/customers";
import type { CautionLevel } from "@/types/database";

const LEVEL_META: Record<
  CautionLevel,
  { label: string; badgeClass: string }
> = {
  none: { label: "騾壼ｸｸ", badgeClass: "bg-navy/5 text-navy/40" },
  caution: { label: "笞・・豕ｨ諢・, badgeClass: "bg-warn/15 text-warn" },
  banned: { label: "笵・蜃ｺ遖・, badgeClass: "bg-danger/15 text-danger" },
};

export function CautionToggle({
  customerId,
  level,
  reason,
  registeredAt,
  registeredByName,
}: {
  customerId: string;
  level: CautionLevel;
  reason: string | null;
  registeredAt: string | null;
  registeredByName: string | null;
}) {
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [pickingLevel, setPickingLevel] = useState<"caution" | "banned" | null>(null);
  const [reasonInput, setReasonInput] = useState("");
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  function submit(next: CautionLevel, reasonText: string | null) {
    setError(null);
    startTransition(async () => {
      try {
        await setCautionAction(customerId, next, reasonText);
        setPickingLevel(null);
        setReasonInput("");
      } catch (err) {
        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "螟画峩縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・);
      }
    });
  }

  return (
    <div className="rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 p-3">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 mb-2">
        <span className={`text-xs font-bold rounded-full px-2.5 py-1 ${LEVEL_META[level].badgeClass}`}>
          {LEVEL_META[level].label}
        </span>
        {level !== "none" && (
          <button
            type="button"
            disabled={pending}
            onClick={() => submit("none", null)}
            className="text-xs text-navy/40 underline disabled:opacity-40"
          >
            隗｣髯､縺吶ｋ
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {level !== "none" && reason && (
        <div className="text-xs text-navy/60 bg-beige rounded-app p-2 mb-2 whitespace-pre-wrap">
          <p className="font-bold">
            逅・罰・嘴reason}
          </p>
          {registeredAt && (
            <p className="text-navy/40 mt-1">
              逋ｻ骭ｲ譌･・嘴new Date(registeredAt).toLocaleDateString("ja-JP")}
              {registeredByName ? `繝ｻ逋ｻ骭ｲ閠・ｼ・{registeredByName}` : ""}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {pickingLevel ? (
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
          <textarea
            value={reasonInput}
            onChange={(e) => setReasonInput(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            placeholder={pickingLevel === "banned" ? "蜃ｺ遖∫炊逕ｱ" : "豕ｨ諢冗炊逕ｱ"}
            className="w-full rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 py-2 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
          />
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <button
              type="button"
              disabled={pending}
              onClick={() => submit(pickingLevel, reasonInput.trim() || null)}
              className="btn-base flex-1 min-h-10 bg-danger text-white text-sm disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {pending ? "菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ窶ｦ" : "菫晏ｭ倥☆繧・}
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setPickingLevel(null)}
              className="btn-base flex-1 min-h-10 bg-white border-2 border-navy/10 text-navy/60 text-sm"
            >
              繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <button
            type="button"
            disabled={pending}
            onClick={() => setPickingLevel("caution")}
            className="btn-base flex-1 min-h-10 bg-warn/10 text-warn border-2 border-warn/30 text-xs font-bold disabled:opacity-50 inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-1"
          >
            <AlertTriangle size={14} /> 豕ｨ諢上↓縺吶ｋ
          </button>
          <button
            type="button"
            disabled={pending}
            onClick={() => setPickingLevel("banned")}
            className="btn-base flex-1 min-h-10 bg-danger/10 text-danger border-2 border-danger/30 text-xs font-bold disabled:opacity-50 inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-1"
          >
            <Ban size={14} /> 蜃ｺ遖√↓縺吶ｋ
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
      {error && <p className="text-danger text-xs font-bold mt-2">{error}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\ChampagneAddForm.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useActionState, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { addChampagneAction } from "@/lib/actions/bottles";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/Button";

const CHAMPAGNE_CANDIDATES = [
  "繝｢繧ｨ 繝悶Μ繝･繝・ヨ",
  "繝｢繧ｨ 繝ｭ繧ｼ",
  "繝峨Φ繝壹Μ 繝悶Μ繝･繝・ヨ",
  "繝峨Φ繝壹Μ 繝ｭ繧ｼ",
  "繝ｭ繝ｼ繝ｩ繝ｳ繝壹Μ繧ｨ",
  "繧ｯ繝ｪ繝･繝・げ",
  "繝ｴ繝ｼ繝ｴ繧ｯ繝ｪ繧ｳ",
  "繝昴Ν繝ｭ繧ｸ繧ｧ",
  "繝・ち繝ｳ繧ｸ繧ｧ",
  "繝懊Λ繝ｳ繧ｸ繧ｧ",
];

const initialState = { error: null };

export function ChampagneAddForm({ customerId }: { customerId: string }) {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [state, formAction, pending] = useActionState(addChampagneAction, initialState);
  const [name, setName] = useState("");
  const formRef = useRef<HTMLFormElement>(null);
  const initialStateRef = useRef(state);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (state !== initialStateRef.current && !state.error) {
      formRef.current?.reset();
      setName("");
      setOpen(false);
    }
  }, [state]);

  if (!open) {
    return (
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => setOpen(true)}
        className="btn-base w-full mt-3 bg-[#7a4fa3] text-white"
      >
        裟 繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ霑ｽ蜉
      </button>
    );
  }

  return (
    <form ref={formRef} action={formAction} className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-3 border-t border-navy/10 pt-3">
      <input type="hidden" name="customer_id" value={customerId} />

      <p className="text-xs font-bold text-[#7a4fa3]">裟 繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ逋ｻ骭ｲ</p>

      {/* 蛟呵｣懊・繧ｿ繝ｳ */}
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
        {CHAMPAGNE_CANDIDATES.map((c) => (
          <button
            key={c}
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setName(c)}
            className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold border transition-colors ${
              name === c
                ? "bg-[#7a4fa3] border-[#7a4fa3] text-white"
                : "bg-white border-navy/10 text-navy/50 hover:bg-navy/5"
            }`}
          >
            {c}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* 蜷榊燕・域焔蜈･蜉帛庄・・*/}
      <input
        type="text"
        name="champagne_name"
        value={name}
        onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ蜷搾ｼ亥呵｣懊↓縺ｪ縺・ｴ蜷医・謇句・蜉幢ｼ・
        className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-[#7a4fa3]"
        required
      />

      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
        <label className="block">
          <span className="block text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-1">譛ｬ謨ｰ</span>
          <input
            type="number"
            name="champagne_quantity"
            min={1}
            defaultValue={1}
            className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
          />
        </label>
        <label className="block col-span-2">
          <span className="block text-xs font-bold text-navy/50 mb-1">驥鷹｡搾ｼ亥・繝ｻ螢ｲ荳翫↓險井ｸ奇ｼ・/span>
          <input
            type="number"
            name="champagne_amount"
            min={0}
            step={1000}
            defaultValue={0}
            placeholder="萓具ｼ・0000"
            className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
          />
        </label>
      </div>

      <input
        type="text"
        name="champagne_memo"
        placeholder="繝｡繝｢・井ｻｻ諢擾ｼ・
        className="w-full min-h-11 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-sm text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
      />

      {state.error && <p className="text-danger text-xs font-bold">{state.error}</p>}

      <div className="flex gap-2">
        <Button type="submit" variant="navy" fullWidth disabled={pending}>
          {pending ? "霑ｽ蜉荳ｭ窶ｦ" : "霑ｽ蜉"}
        </Button>
        <Button type="button" variant="outline" onClick={() => setOpen(false)}>
          髢峨§繧・        </Button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\CustomerCard.tsx ---

import Link from "next/link";
import type { CustomerWithMonthStats } from "@/types/database";
import { Card } from "@/components/ui/Card";
import { LinkButton } from "@/components/ui/Button";
import { RankBadge } from "./RankBadge";
import { FavoriteToggle } from "./FavoriteToggle";
import { daysSince, yen } from "@/lib/date";
import { computePace } from "@/lib/pace";

export function CustomerCard({
  customer,
  secondaryAction = "reservation",
}: {
  customer: CustomerWithMonthStats;
  secondaryAction?: "reservation" | "detail";
}) {
  const pace = computePace(customer);
  return (
    <Card className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center gap-3 sm:gap-6">
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap mb-1">
          <Link
            href={`/customers/${customer.id}`}
            className="text-lg font-black text-navy hover:underline"
          >
            {customer.display_name}
          </Link>
          <FavoriteToggle customerId={customer.id} favorite={customer.favorite} size={16} />
          <RankBadge rank={customer.rank} />
          {customer.caution_level === "banned" && (
            <span className="text-[11px] font-bold text-white bg-danger rounded-full px-2 py-0.5">
              笵・蜃ｺ遖・            </span>
          )}
          {customer.caution_level === "caution" && (
            <span className="text-[11px] font-bold text-white bg-warn rounded-full px-2 py-0.5">
              笞・・豕ｨ諢・            </span>
          )}
          {customer.tags.map((t) => (
            <span
              key={t.id}
              className="text-[11px] font-bold text-navy/50 bg-navy/5 rounded-full px-2 py-0.5"
            >
              {t.name}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-x-4 gap-y-1 text-sm text-navy/60">
          <span>
            譚･蠎養customer.visit_count}蝗・/ 莉頑怦{customer.month_visit_count}蝗・          </span>
          <span>
            譛邨・            {customer.last_visit_at ? `${daysSince(customer.last_visit_at)}譌･蜑港 : "譚･蠎励↑縺・}
          </span>
          <span className="font-bold text-navy">
            莉頑怦螢ｲ荳・{yen(customer.month_amount)}
          </span>
          {customer.current_bottle_count > 0 && (
            <span className="text-warn font-bold">
              差{customer.current_bottle_count}譛ｬ
            </span>
          )}
          {pace.label !== "-" && (
            <span className="text-success font-bold">譚･蠎励・繝ｼ繧ｹ・嘴pace.label}</span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 shrink-0">
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <LinkButton href={`/visits/new?customer=${customer.id}`} variant="gold" className="px-4">
            譚･蠎・          </LinkButton>
          {secondaryAction === "reservation" ? (
            <LinkButton href={`/reservations?customer=${customer.id}`} variant="navy" className="px-4">
              莠育ｴ・            </LinkButton>
          ) : (
            <LinkButton href={`/customers/${customer.id}`} variant="navy" className="px-4">
              隧ｳ邏ｰ
            </LinkButton>
          )}
        </div>
        <a
          href={`/customers/${customer.id}/edit`}
          className="text-center text-xs text-navy/40 underline hover:text-navy/60"
        >
          隱慕函譌･繝ｻ邱ｨ髮・        </a>
      </div>
    </Card>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\CustomerEditForm.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useTransition } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { updateCustomerAction } from "@/lib/actions/customers";
import { TextField } from "@/components/ui/TextField";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/Button";
import type { Customer } from "@/types/database";

export function CustomerEditForm({ customer }: { customer: Customer }) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [displayName, setDisplayName] = useState(customer.display_name);
  const [kana, setKana] = useState(customer.kana ?? "");
  const [realName, setRealName] = useState(customer.real_name ?? "");
  const [birthday, setBirthday] = useState(customer.birthday ?? "");
  const [memo, setMemo] = useState(customer.memo ?? "");

  function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!displayName.trim()) {
      setError("逋ｻ骭ｲ蜷阪ｒ蜈･蜉帙＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・);
      return;
    }
    setError(null);
    startTransition(async () => {
      try {
        await updateCustomerAction(customer.id, {
          display_name: displayName.trim(),
          kana: kana.trim(),
          real_name: realName.trim(),
          birthday,
          memo: memo.trim(),
        });
        router.push(`/customers/${customer.id}`);
      } catch (err) {
        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "譖ｴ譁ｰ縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・);
      }
    });
  }

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex flex-col gap-4">
      <TextField
        label="逋ｻ骭ｲ蜷搾ｼ亥ｿ・茨ｼ・
        value={displayName}
        onChange={(e) => setDisplayName(e.target.value)}
        required
      />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <TextField label="縺ｵ繧翫′縺ｪ" value={kana} onChange={(e) => setKana(e.target.value)} />
        <TextField label="譛ｬ蜷搾ｼ井ｻｻ諢擾ｼ・ value={realName} onChange={(e) => setRealName(e.target.value)} />
      </div>
      <div>
        <span className="block text-sm font-bold text-navy/70 mb-1.5">隱慕函譌･・域怦繝ｻ譌･縺ｮ縺ｿ・・/span>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <select
            value={birthday.slice(5, 7) || ""}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const d = birthday.slice(8, 10) || "01";
              setBirthday(e.target.value ? `2000-${e.target.value}-${d}` : "");
            }}
            className="min-h-12 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-base text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
          >
            <option value="">譛医ｒ驕ｸ謚・/option>
            {Array.from({ length: 12 }, (_, i) => i + 1).map((mn) => (
              <option key={mn} value={String(mn).padStart(2, "0")}>{mn}譛・/option>
            ))}
          </select>
          <select
            value={birthday.slice(8, 10) || ""}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const mo = birthday.slice(5, 7) || "01";
              setBirthday(e.target.value ? `2000-${mo}-${e.target.value}` : "");
            }}
            className="min-h-12 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 text-base text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
          >
            <option value="">譌･繧帝∈謚・/option>
            {Array.from({ length: 31 }, (_, i) => i + 1).map((dd) => (
              <option key={dd} value={String(dd).padStart(2, "0")}>{dd}譌･</option>
            ))}
          </select>
          {birthday && (
            <button type="button" onClick={() => setBirthday("")} className="text-navy/30 text-sm underline">
              繧ｯ繝ｪ繧｢
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      <label className="block">
        <span className="block text-sm font-bold text-navy/70 mb-1.5">繝｡繝｢</span>
        <textarea
          value={memo}
          onChange={(e) => setMemo(e.target.value)}
          rows={3}
          className="w-full rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-base text-navy focus:outline-none focus:border-gold"
        />
      </label>
      {error && <p className="text-danger text-sm font-bold">{error}</p>}
      <div className="flex gap-3">
        <Button type="submit" variant="gold" disabled={pending} fullWidth>
          {pending ? "菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ窶ｦ" : "菫晏ｭ・}
        </Button>
        <Button
          type="button"
          variant="outline"
          onClick={() => router.push(`/customers/${customer.id}`)}
        >
          繧ｭ繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ
        </Button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\CustomerSearchBar.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { useRouter, usePathname, useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { Search } from "lucide-react";

type Props = {
  placeholder: string;
  paramName?: string;
};

/**
 * 蜈･蜉帙↓蠢懊§縺ｦURL縺ｮ讀懃ｴ｢繧ｯ繧ｨ繝ｪ繧呈峩譁ｰ縺吶ｋ・育ｬｬ9遶縲後Μ繧｢繝ｫ繧ｿ繧､繝讀懃ｴ｢縲搾ｼ峨・ * 300ms繝・ヰ繧ｦ繝ｳ繧ｹ縺励※驕ｷ遘ｻ縺吶ｋ縺薙→縺ｧ縲√し繝ｼ繝舌・蜀肴､懃ｴ｢縺ｮ鬆ｻ蠎ｦ繧呈椛縺医▽縺､
 * 菴捺─騾溷ｺｦ繧堤ｶｭ謖√☆繧具ｼ育ｬｬ35遶 讀懃ｴ｢300ms莉･蜀・ｼ峨・ */
export function CustomerSearchBar({ placeholder, paramName = "q" }: Props) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const [value, setValue] = useState(searchParams.get(paramName) ?? "");
  const timerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (timerRef.current) clearTimeout(timerRef.current);
    timerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
      const params = new URLSearchParams(searchParams.toString());
      if (value.trim()) {
        params.set(paramName, value.trim());
      } else {
        params.delete(paramName);
      }
      params.delete("page");
      router.push(`${pathname}?${params.toString()}`);
    }, 300);
    return () => {
      if (timerRef.current) clearTimeout(timerRef.current);
    };
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [value]);

  return (
    <div className="relative">
      <Search
        size={20}
        className="absolute left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-navy/30"
      />
      <input
        value={value}
        onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)}
        placeholder={placeholder}
        className="w-full min-h-14 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white pl-12 pr-4 text-base text-navy placeholder:text-navy/30 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold transition-colors"
      />
    </div>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\CustomerTimeline.tsx ---

import { Card, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/Card";
import { formatDate } from "@/lib/date";
import type { TimelineEvent } from "@/lib/data/timeline";

const KIND_META: Record<TimelineEvent["kind"], { emoji: string; color: string }> = {
  first_visit: { emoji: "脂", color: "text-gold" },
  visit: { emoji: "査", color: "text-success" },
  bottle: { emoji: "差", color: "text-warn" },
  reservation: { emoji: "套", color: "text-info" },
  note: { emoji: "統", color: "text-navy/50" },
  champagne: { emoji: "･・, color: "text-[#7a4fa3]" },
};

/** 鬘ｧ螳｢繧ｿ繧､繝繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ・医Ξ繝薙Η繝ｼ謖・遭竭ｫ・会ｼ壽擂蠎励・繝懊ヨ繝ｫ繝ｻ莠育ｴ・・繝｡繝｢繧呈凾邉ｻ蛻励〒陦ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ縲・*/
export function CustomerTimeline({ events }: { events: TimelineEvent[] }) {
  return (
    <Card>
      <CardTitle>繧ｿ繧､繝繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ</CardTitle>
      {events.length === 0 && (
        <p className="text-navy/40 text-sm">縺ｾ縺螻･豁ｴ縺後≠繧翫∪縺帙ｓ縲・/p>
      )}
      <ul className="flex flex-col max-h-[500px] overflow-y-auto">
        {events.map((e, i) => {
          const meta = KIND_META[e.kind];
          return (
            <li key={e.id} className="flex gap-3">
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center">
                <span className="text-lg leading-none mt-0.5">{meta.emoji}</span>
                {i < events.length - 1 && <span className="flex-1 w-px bg-navy/10 my-1" />}
              </div>
              <div className="pb-4 min-w-0">
                <p className="text-xs text-navy/40">{formatDate(e.date)}</p>
                <p className={`text-sm font-bold ${meta.color}`}>{e.title}</p>
                {e.detail && (
                  <p className="text-xs text-navy/50 truncate max-w-xs">{e.detail}</p>
                )}
              </div>
            </li>
          );
        })}
      </ul>
    </Card>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\FavoriteStars.tsx ---

import { Star } from "lucide-react";

/** 縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧奇ｼ育ｬｬ25遶・峨０N/OFF縺ｮ縺ｿ縺ｧ縲＾N縺ｮ縺ｨ縺阪□縺鯛・繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ・郁ｪｭ縺ｿ蜿悶ｊ蟆ら畑縺ｮ陦ｨ遉ｺ邂・園縺ｧ菴ｿ逕ｨ・峨・*/
export function FavoriteStars({ favorite, size = 14 }: { favorite: boolean; size?: number }) {
  if (!favorite) return null;
  return (
    <span className="inline-flex text-gold" aria-label="縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧・>
      <Star size={size} fill="currentColor" strokeWidth={0} />
    </span>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\FavoriteToggle.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState, useTransition } from "react";
import { Star } from "lucide-react";
import { toggleFavoriteAction } from "@/lib/actions/customers";

/**
 * 縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧奇ｼ育ｬｬ25遶・峨０N/OFF縺ｮ縺ｿ縲∵弌1縺､縺ｧ陦ｨ迴ｾ縺吶ｋ縲・ *
 * RC4菫ｮ豁｣: 縺薙ｌ縺ｾ縺ｧ繝ｭ繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｫstate縺ｨ繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・縺ｮ蛟､縺碁｣溘＞驕輔＞縲∽ｸ隕ｧ蜀・・蛻･縺ｮ鬘ｧ螳｢縺ｮ
 * 譏溘′隱､縺｣縺ｦ轤ｹ轣ｯ縺吶ｋ繧医≧縺ｫ隕九∴繧倶ｸ榊・蜷医′縺ゅ▲縺溘ゅΟ繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｫ縺ｫ迢ｬ閾ｪ縺ｮ逵溷⊃蛟､繧・ * 謖√◆縺壹∝ｸｸ縺ｫ繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・縺九ｉ貂｡縺輔ｌ縺・favorite 縺ｮ蛟､繧偵◎縺ｮ縺ｾ縺ｾ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ縺薙→縺ｧ縲・ * 陦ｨ遉ｺ縺ｮ繧ｺ繝ｬ縺瑚ｵｷ縺阪↑縺・ｈ縺・↓縺励◆縲・ *
 * RC5菫ｮ豁｣: 荳隕ｧ縺ｮ荳ｦ縺ｳ鬆・′ last_visit_at 縺ｮ蜷悟､繧ｿ繧､繝悶Ξ繝ｼ繧ｯ縺ｧ荳榊ｮ牙ｮ壹□縺｣縺溷撫鬘後・
 * 繝・・繧ｿ蜿門ｾ怜・・・istCustomers・峨〒隗｣豸域ｸ医∩縲ゅ％縺薙〒縺ｯ蛻・ｊ譖ｿ縺育峩蠕後↓荳險豺ｻ縺医※縲・ * 逕ｻ髱｢縺梧･縺ｫ螟峨ｏ縺｣縺溘ｈ縺・↓諢溘§縺ｪ縺・ｈ縺・↓縺吶ｋ縲・ */
export function FavoriteToggle({
  customerId,
  favorite,
  size = 20,
}: {
  customerId: string;
  favorite: boolean;
  size?: number;
}) {
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [justChanged, setJustChanged] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!justChanged) return;
    const timer = setTimeout(() => setJustChanged(false), 1500);
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [justChanged]);

  return (
    <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1">
      <button
        type="button"
        disabled={pending}
        onClick={() =>
          startTransition(async () => {
            await toggleFavoriteAction(customerId, !favorite);
            setJustChanged(true);
          })
        }
        aria-pressed={favorite}
        aria-label={favorite ? "縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧翫ｒ隗｣髯､" : "縺頑ｰ励↓蜈･繧翫↓霑ｽ蜉"}
        className="inline-flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50"
      >
        <Star
          size={size}
          className={favorite ? "text-gold" : "text-navy/25"}
          fill={favorite ? "currentColor" : "none"}
          strokeWidth={1.75}
        />
      </button>
      {justChanged && (
        <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-navy/40">螟画峩縺励∪縺励◆</span>
      )}
    </span>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\HideCustomerButton.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useTransition } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { setCustomerHiddenAction } from "@/lib/actions/customers";

export function HideCustomerButton({
  customerId,
  hidden,
}: {
  customerId: string;
  hidden: boolean;
}) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();

  function handleClick() {
    const confirmMsg = hidden
      ? "縺薙・鬘ｧ螳｢繧貞ｾｩ蜈・＠縺ｾ縺吶°・・
      : "縺薙・鬘ｧ螳｢繧堤┌蜉ｹ蛹厄ｼ磯撼陦ｨ遉ｺ・峨＠縺ｾ縺吶°・溘ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ縺ｯ蜑企勁縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲ゆｸ隕ｧ繝ｻ讀懃ｴ｢縺九ｉ隕九∴縺ｪ縺上↑繧翫∪縺吶・;
    if (!confirm(confirmMsg)) return;
    startTransition(async () => {
      await setCustomerHiddenAction(customerId, !hidden);
      router.refresh();
    });
  }

  return (
    <button
      type="button"
      disabled={pending}
      onClick={handleClick}
      className="text-xs text-navy/40 underline disabled:opacity-40"
    >
      {hidden ? "蠕ｩ蜈・☆繧・ : "縺薙・鬘ｧ螳｢繧堤┌蜉ｹ蛹・}
    </button>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\customers\InvalidateNoteButton.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useTransition } from "react";
import { invalidateNoteAction } from "@/lib/actions/notes";

export function InvalidateNoteButton({
  noteId,
  customerId,
}: {
  noteId: string;
  customerId: string;
}) {
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();

  return (
    <button
      type="button"
      disabled={pending}
      onClick={() => {
        if (confirm("縺薙・繝｡繝｢繧堤┌蜉ｹ蛹悶＠縺ｾ縺吶°・滂ｼ域悽譁・・菫晄戟縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺吶′荳隕ｧ縺九ｉ髱櫁｡ｨ遉ｺ縺ｫ縺ｪ繧翫∪縺呻ｼ・)) {
          startTransition(() => invalidateNoteAction(noteId, customerId));
        }
      }}
      className="text-navy/30 text-xs underline disabled:opacity-40 shrink-0"
    >
      辟｡蜉ｹ蛹・    </button>
  );
}

--- filename: \src\components\customers\NoteForm.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useActionState, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { addNoteAction, type AddNoteState } from "@/lib/actions/notes";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/Button";
import { enqueueWrite } from "@/lib/offline/queue";

const initialState: AddNoteState = { error: null };

export function NoteForm({ customerId }: { customerId: string }) {
  const [state, formAction, pending] = useActionState(addNoteAction, initialState);
  const [offlineMessage, setOfflineMessage] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const textareaRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);
  // RC3菫ｮ豁｣: action={formAction} 繧堤峩謗･貂｡縺呎ｨ呎ｺ悶ヱ繧ｿ繝ｼ繝ｳ縺ｫ邨ｱ荳縺吶ｋ
  // ・・ction繧偵Λ繝・・縺励※formAction繧貞・驛ｨ縺ｧ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺呎婿蠑上・驕ｿ縺代ｋ・峨・  const initialStateRef = useRef(state);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (state !== initialStateRef.current && !state.error && textareaRef.current) {
      textareaRef.current.value = "";
    }
  }, [state]);

  async function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) {
    if (typeof navigator === "undefined" || navigator.onLine) {
      setOfflineMessage(null);
      return; // 繧ｪ繝ｳ繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ: action={formAction} 縺ｫ縺昴・縺ｾ縺ｾ莉ｻ縺帙ｋ
    }

    // 隨ｬ38遶: 繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ譎ゅ・遶ｯ譛ｫ縺ｫ荳譎ゆｿ晏ｭ倥＠縲∝ｾｩ譌ｧ蠕後↓SyncManager縺瑚・蜍暮∽ｿ｡縺吶ｋ
    e.preventDefault();
    const formData = new FormData(e.currentTarget);
    await enqueueWrite("note", formData);
    setOfflineMessage("繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ縺ｮ縺溘ａ遶ｯ譛ｫ縺ｫ菫晏ｭ倥＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲ょｾｩ譌ｧ蠕後↓閾ｪ蜍暮∽ｿ｡縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺吶・);
    if (textareaRef.current) textareaRef.current.value = "";
  }

  return (
    <form action={formAction} onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-3">
      <input type="hidden" name="customer_id" value={customerId} />
      <textarea
        ref={textareaRef}
        name="note"
        rows={2}
        placeholder="繝｡繝｢繧定ｿｽ蜉・井ｸ頑嶌縺阪〒縺ｯ縺ｪ縺剰ｿｽ蜉縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺呻ｼ・
        className="w-full rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-3 py-2 text-sm text-navy placeholder:text-navy/30 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold transition-colors"
      />
      {state.error && <p className="text-danger text-xs font-bold">{state.error}</p>}
      {offlineMessage && <p className="text-warn text-xs font-bold">{offlineMessage}</p>}
      <Button type="submit" variant="outline" disabled={pending} className="self-end px-4 min-h-10">
        {pending ? "霑ｽ蜉荳ｭ窶ｦ" : "繝｡繝｢繧定ｿｽ蜉"}
      </Button>
    </form>
  );
}

import type { CustomerRank } from "@/types/database";

const RANK_LABEL: Record<CustomerRank, string> = {
  first: "蛻晄擂蠎・,
  regular: "蟶ｸ騾｣",
  vip: "VIP",
  special: "迚ｹ蛻･",
};

const RANK_CLASS: Record<CustomerRank, string> = {
  first: "bg-navy/10 text-navy/60",
  regular: "bg-gold/20 text-gold-dark",
  vip: "bg-[#efe4f7] text-[#7a4fa3]",
  special: "bg-[#fde7d4] text-warn",
};

export function RankBadge({ rank }: { rank: CustomerRank }) {
  return (
    <span
      className={`inline-flex items-center px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold ${RANK_CLASS[rank]}`}

--- filename: \src\components\customers\RankSelector.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useState, useTransition } from "react";
import { updateCustomerRankAction } from "@/lib/actions/customers";
import type { CustomerRank } from "@/types/database";

const OPTIONS: { value: CustomerRank; label: string }[] = [
  { value: "first", label: "蛻晄擂蠎・ },
  { value: "regular", label: "蟶ｸ騾｣" },
  { value: "vip", label: "VIP" },
  { value: "special", label: "迚ｹ蛻･" },
];

export function RankSelector({
  customerId,
  currentRank,
}: {
  customerId: string;
  currentRank: CustomerRank;
}) {
  const [rank, setRank] = useState(currentRank);
  const [pending, startTransition] = useTransition();
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <select
        value={rank}
        disabled={pending}
        onChange={(e) => {
          const next = e.target.value as CustomerRank;
          setRank(next);
          setError(null);
          startTransition(async () => {
            try {
              await updateCustomerRankAction(customerId, next);
            } catch (err) {
              setRank(currentRank);
              setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "螟画峩縺ｫ螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲・);
            }
          });
        }}
        className="min-h-9 rounded-app border-2 border-navy/10 bg-white px-2 text-xs font-bold text-navy"
      >
        {OPTIONS.map((o) => (
          <option key={o.value} value={o.value}>
            {o.label}
          </option>
        ))}
      </select>
      {error && <span className="text-danger text-xs font-bold">{error}</span>}
    </div>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\dashboard\MonthlyLineChart.tsx ---

"use client";

import {
  ComposedChart,
  Line,
  XAxis,
  YAxis,
  CartesianGrid,
  Tooltip,
  Legend,
  ResponsiveContainer,
} from "recharts";
import type { MonthlyGraphData } from "@/lib/data/dashboard";

function formatYen(n: number): string {
  if (n >= 10000) return `${Math.floor(n / 10000)}荳㌔;
  return `ﾂ･${n.toLocaleString("ja-JP")}`;
}

const DATA_KEY_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  thisYearAmount: "莉雁ｹｴ螢ｲ荳・,
  lastYearAmount: "譏ｨ蟷ｴ螢ｲ荳・,
  thisYearPeople: "譚･蠎嶺ｺｺ謨ｰ",
};

export function MonthlyLineChart({ data }: { data: MonthlyGraphData[] }) {
  return (
    <div>
      <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={230}>
        <ComposedChart data={data} margin={{ top: 8, right: 44, left: -16, bottom: 0 }}>
          <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#e5e7eb" />
          <XAxis
            dataKey="month"
            tickFormatter={(v: unknown) => `${v}譛・}
            tick={{ fontSize: 11, fill: "#6b7280" }}
          />
          {/* 蟾ｦY霆ｸ: 螢ｲ荳奇ｼ亥・・・*/}
          <YAxis
            yAxisId="amount"
            orientation="left"
            tickFormatter={formatYen}
            tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#6b7280" }}
            width={50}
          />
          {/* 蜿ｳY霆ｸ: 譚･蠎嶺ｺｺ謨ｰ・井ｺｺ・・*/}
          <YAxis
            yAxisId="people"
            orientation="right"
            tickFormatter={(v: unknown) => `${v}莠ｺ`}
            tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#16a34a" }}
            width={40}
          />
          <Tooltip
            formatter={(value: unknown, dataKey: unknown) => {
              const key = String(dataKey);
              const num = Number(value);
              if (key === "thisYearPeople") {
                return [`${num}莠ｺ`, DATA_KEY_LABELS[key] ?? key];
              }
              return [`ﾂ･${num.toLocaleString("ja-JP")}`, DATA_KEY_LABELS[key] ?? key];
            }}
            labelFormatter={(v: unknown) => `${v}譛・}
          />
          <Legend
            formatter={(value: string) => DATA_KEY_LABELS[value] ?? value}
            wrapperStyle={{ fontSize: 12 }}
          />
          <Line
            yAxisId="amount"
            type="monotone"
            dataKey="thisYearAmount"
            stroke="#2563eb"
            strokeWidth={2}
            dot={{ r: 3 }}
            activeDot={{ r: 5 }}
          />
          <Line
            yAxisId="amount"
            type="monotone"
            dataKey="lastYearAmount"
            stroke="#dc2626"
            strokeWidth={2}
            dot={{ r: 3 }}
            activeDot={{ r: 5 }}
            strokeDasharray="4 2"
          />
          <Line
            yAxisId="people"
            type="monotone"
            dataKey="thisYearPeople"
            stroke="#16a34a"
            strokeWidth={2}
            dot={{ r: 3 }}
            activeDot={{ r: 5 }}
          />
        </ComposedChart>
      </ResponsiveContainer>
    </div>
  );
}

--- filename: \src\components\layout\BottomNav.tsx ---

"use client";

import Link from "next/link";
import Image from "next/image";
import { usePathname } from "next/navigation";
import { NAV_ITEMS } from "./nav-items";
import type { StaffRole } from "@/types/database";

export function BottomNav({ role }: { role: StaffRole }) {
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const items = NAV_ITEMS.filter((item) => !item.adminOnly || role === "admin");

  return (
    <nav className="md:hidden fixed bottom-0 inset-x-0 z-20 bg-white border-t border-navy/10 flex pb-[env(safe-area-inset-bottom)]">
      {items.map((item) => {
        const active = pathname === item.href || pathname.startsWith(item.href + "/");
        const Icon   = item.icon;
        return (
          <Link
            key={item.href}
            href={item.href}
            prefetch={true}
            className={`flex-1 min-w-0 min-h-14 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-0.5 text-[10px] font-bold px-0.5 ${
              active ? "text-navy" : "text-navy/40"
            }`}
          >
            {/* MATTY繧｢繧､繧ｳ繝ｳ・育判蜒擾ｼ峨∪縺溘・Lucide繧｢繧､繧ｳ繝ｳ */}
            {item.imageSrc ? (
              <Image
                src={item.imageSrc}
                alt={item.label}
                width={22}
                height={22}
                className={active ? "opacity-100" : "opacity-40"}
              />
            ) : Icon ? (
              <Icon size={20} strokeWidth={active ? 2.5 : 2} />
            ) : null}
            <span className="truncate max-w-full">{item.shortLabel ?? item.label}</span>
          </Link>
        );
      })}
    </nav>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\layout\CustomerCacheSyncManager.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useEffect } from "react";
import { syncCustomerCache } from "@/lib/offline/customer-cache";

const BACKGROUND_REFRESH_MS = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5蛻・＃縺ｨ縺ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ繧ｰ繝ｩ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝画峩譁ｰ・育ｬｬ38遶隕∽ｻｶ・・
/**
 * 鬘ｧ螳｢讀懃ｴ｢繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･・・ndexedDB・峨ｒ繝舌ャ繧ｯ繧ｰ繝ｩ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝峨〒譛譁ｰ縺ｫ菫昴▽縲・ * 襍ｷ蜍墓凾繝ｻ繧ｪ繝ｳ繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ蠕ｩ蟶ｰ譎ゅ・5蛻・＃縺ｨ縺ｫ縲∵怙霑鷹夢隕ｧ繝ｻ譚･蠎励＠縺滓怙螟ｧ1000莉ｶ繧貞酔譛溘☆繧九・ */
export function CustomerCacheSyncManager() {
  useEffect(() => {
    void syncCustomerCache();
    window.addEventListener("online", syncCustomerCache);
    const interval = setInterval(() => void syncCustomerCache(), BACKGROUND_REFRESH_MS);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener("online", syncCustomerCache);
      clearInterval(interval);
    };
  }, []);

  return null;
}



--- filename: \src\components\layout\Header.tsx ---

import Image from "next/image";
import { logout } from "@/lib/auth/actions";
import { toJstDateString } from "@/lib/date";

type HeaderProps = {
  title: string;
  staffName: string;
};

/** 莉､蜥悟ｹｴ螟画鋤・郁･ｿ證ｦ竊剃ｻ､蜥鯉ｼ・*/
function toReiwa(year: number): string {
  const reiwa = year - 2018;
  if (reiwa <= 0) return `${year}`;
  return `莉､蜥・{reiwa}蟷ｴ`;
}

/** 譌･莉倥ヰ繝ｼ逕ｨ: 縲・026蟷ｴ(莉､蜥・蟷ｴ)7譛・譌･(譛・縲榊ｽ｢蠑・*/
function formatDateBar(isoDateStr: string): string {
  const WEEKDAY_JA = ["譌･", "譛・, "轣ｫ", "豌ｴ", "譛ｨ", "驥・, "蝨・];
  const [y, m, d] = isoDateStr.split("-").map(Number);
  const date = new Date(y, m - 1, d);
  const dow = WEEKDAY_JA[date.getDay()];
  return `${y}蟷ｴ(${toReiwa(y)})${m}譛・{d}譌･(${dow})`;
}

/**
 * 逕ｻ髱｢荳企Κ縺ｮ蜈ｱ騾壹・繝・ム繝ｼ縲・ * 閭梧勹騾城℃迚・ATTY繧｢繧､繧ｳ繝ｳ + 繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ荳九↓譛ｬ譌･縺ｮ譌･莉倥ヰ繝ｼ繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縲・ */
export function Header({ title, staffName }: HeaderProps) {
  const todayStr = toJstDateString(new Date().toISOString());
  const dateLabel = formatDateBar(todayStr);

  return (
    <div className="shrink-0">
      {/* 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繝倥ャ繝繝ｼ */}
      <header className="bg-gold text-navy-dark min-h-[68px] flex items-center justify-between px-4 md:px-6 border-b border-black/10 py-1.5">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
          {/* 閭梧勹騾城℃繧｢繧､繧ｳ繝ｳ: 鮟・牡閭梧勹縺ｨ鬥ｴ譟薙・ */}
          <Image
            src="/icons/matty-transparent-96.png"
            alt=""
            width={68}
            height={68}
            className="shrink-0"
          />
          <span className="font-black text-xl tracking-tight shrink-0">MATTY</span>
          <span className="text-navy-dark/60 text-sm truncate hidden sm:inline pl-1">
            {title}
          </span>
        </div>
        <form action={logout} className="flex items-center gap-3 shrink-0">
          <span className="text-sm text-navy-dark/70 hidden sm:inline">
            {staffName}
          </span>
          <button
            type="submit"
            className="text-sm font-bold text-navy-dark border border-navy-dark/30 rounded-app px-3 py-2 hover:bg-black/5"
          >
            繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝・          </button>
        </form>
      </header>

      {/* 譌･莉倥ヰ繝ｼ: 閭梧勹縺ｪ縺励・譁・ｭ励・縺ｿ */}
      <div className="py-1 text-center border-b border-black/5">
        <p className="text-navy-dark/80 font-bold text-sm md:text-base tracking-wide">
          {dateLabel}
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

--- filename: \src\components\layout\OfflineBanner.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useOnlineStatus } from "@/lib/offline/useOnlineStatus";
import { subscribePendingCount } from "@/lib/offline/queue";

/** 隨ｬ38遶:縲後が繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ荳ｭ縺ｯ逕ｻ髱｢荳企Κ縺ｸ縲弱が繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ縲上→陦ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ縲・*/
export function OfflineBanner() {
  const online = useOnlineStatus();
  const [pendingCount, setPendingCount] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => subscribePendingCount(setPendingCount), []);

  if (online && pendingCount === 0) return null;

  return (
    <div
      className={`text-center text-xs font-bold py-1.5 px-2 ${
        online ? "bg-success text-white" : "bg-warn text-white"
      }`}
      role="status"
    >
      {online
        ? `菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ縺ｮ繝・・繧ｿ ${pendingCount}莉ｶ繧貞酔譛溘＠縺ｦ縺・∪縺吮ｦ`
        : pendingCount > 0
        ? `繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ・域悴騾∽ｿ｡ ${pendingCount}莉ｶ繝ｻ蠕ｩ譌ｧ蠕後↓閾ｪ蜍募酔譛滂ｼ荏
        : "繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ・亥ｾｩ譌ｧ蠕後↓閾ｪ蜍募酔譛滂ｼ・}
    </div>
  );
}



--- filename: \src\components\layout\ServiceWorkerRegister.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useEffect } from "react";

/**
 * RC3菫ｮ豁｣: 蜿榊ｾｩ繝・せ繝井ｸｭ縺ｫService Worker縺ｮ蜿､縺・く繝｣繝・す繝･縺梧眠縺励＞JS繧定ｦ・＞髫縺励・ * 縲後さ繝ｼ繝峨・逶ｴ縺励◆縺ｮ縺ｫ螳滓ｩ溘・謖吝虚縺悟､峨ｏ繧峨↑縺・榊撫鬘後・貂ｩ蠎翫↓縺ｪ縺｣縺ｦ縺・◆縺溘ａ縲・ * 荳譌ｦPWA縺ｮ繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･讖溯・繧貞ｮ悟・縺ｫ辟｡蜉ｹ蛹悶☆繧具ｼ医く繝ｫ繧ｹ繧､繝・メ・峨・ *
 * 譌｢蟄倥↓繧､繝ｳ繧ｹ繝医・繝ｫ貂医∩縺ｮService Worker縺後≠繧後・遨肴･ｵ逧・↓逋ｻ骭ｲ隗｣髯､縺励・ * Cache Storage繧ょ・豸亥悉縺吶ｋ縲ゅ％繧後↓繧医ｊ驕主悉縺ｮRC縺ｧ逋ｻ骭ｲ縺輔ｌ縺欖W縺・ * 螳滓ｩ溘↓谿九▲縺ｦ縺・※繧ゅ∵ｬ｡蝗槭い繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ譎ゅ↓遒ｺ螳溘↓繧ｯ繝ｪ繧｢縺輔ｌ繧九・ *
 * PWA繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ蟇ｾ蠢懊・蜀肴怏蜉ｹ蛹悶・繧ｳ繧｢讖溯・・井ｿ晏ｭ倥・讀懃ｴ｢・峨・螳牙ｮ壼ｾ後↓
 * 謾ｹ繧√※險ｭ險医☆繧具ｼ・2・峨・ */
export function ServiceWorkerRegister() {
  useEffect(() => {
    if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
    if (!("serviceWorker" in navigator)) return;

    navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistrations().then((registrations) => {
      registrations.forEach((registration) => {
        registration.unregister().catch(() => {
          // 螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｦ繧り・蜻ｽ逧・〒縺ｯ縺ｪ縺・◆繧∫┌隕悶☆繧・        });
      });
    }).catch(() => {
      // no-op
    });

    if (typeof caches !== "undefined") {
      caches.keys().then((keys) => {
        keys.forEach((key) => {
          caches.delete(key).catch(() => {
            // no-op
          });
        });
      }).catch(() => {
        // no-op
      });
    }
  }, []);

  return null;
}
