--- filename: \src\lib\data\timeline.ts ---

import { createClient } from "@/lib/supabase/server";

export type TimelineEvent = {
  id: string;
  date: string; // ISO
  kind: "first_visit" | "visit" | "bottle" | "reservation" | "note" | "champagne";
  title: string;
  detail: string | null;
};

/**
 * 鬘ｧ螳｢繧ｿ繧､繝繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ・医Ξ繝薙Η繝ｼ謖・遭竭ｫ縲ヽC7菫ｮ豁｣竭ｫ竊停贈・峨・ * 譚･蠎励・繝懊ヨ繝ｫ霑ｽ蜉繝ｻ莠育ｴ・・繝｡繝｢霑ｽ蜉繧呈凾邉ｻ蛻励〒邨ｱ蜷医☆繧九・ * RC7菫ｮ豁｣: 莉｣陦ｨ閠・→縺励※縺ｮ譚･蠎励□縺代〒縺ｪ縺上∝酔莨ｴ閠・→縺励※譚･蠎励＠縺滓律繧ょ性繧√ｋ縲・ * 縲悟・蝗樊擂蠎励阪・莉｣陦ｨ閠・蜷御ｼｴ閠・←縺｡繧峨・遶句ｴ縺ｧ繧ゅ∵怙繧ょ商縺・擂蠎玲律繧呈治逕ｨ縺吶ｋ縲・ */
export async function getCustomerTimeline(customerId: string): Promise<TimelineEvent[]> {
  const supabase = await createClient();

  const [
    primaryVisitsRes,
    companionMembershipsRes,
    bottlesRes,
    reservationsRes,
    notesRes,
    champagnesRes,
  ] = await Promise.all([
    supabase
      .from("visits")
      .select("id, visited_at, amount")
      .eq("primary_customer_id", customerId)
      .eq("invalidated", false)
      .order("visited_at", { ascending: true }),
    // RC8菫ｮ豁｣: visit_members竊致isits竊団ustomers 縺ｨ縺・≧3谿ｵ繝阪せ繝医・embed繧ｯ繧ｨ繝ｪ縺ｯ
    // 迺ｰ蠅・↓繧医▲縺ｦ荳榊ｮ牙ｮ壹↑縺溘ａ縲∝腰邏斐↑繧ｯ繧ｨ繝ｪ縺ｫ蛻・ｧ｣縺励※JS蛛ｴ縺ｧ邨仙粋縺吶ｋ
    // ・井ｻ悶・邂・園縺ｧ螳溽ｸｾ縺ｮ縺ゅｋ遒ｺ螳溘↑繝代ち繝ｼ繝ｳ縺ｫ邨ｱ荳・峨・    supabase
      .from("visit_members")
      .select("visit_id")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId)
      .eq("member_type", "companion"),
    supabase
      .from("bottles")
      .select("id, bottle_type, bottle_name, created_at")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId)
      .order("created_at", { ascending: true }),
    supabase
      .from("reservations")
      .select("id, reserved_at, status, created_at")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId)
      .order("created_at", { ascending: true }),
    supabase
      .from("notes")
      .select("id, note, created_at")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId)
      .eq("invalidated", false)
      .order("created_at", { ascending: true }),
    supabase
      .from("champagnes")
      .select("id, name, created_at")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId)
      .order("created_at", { ascending: true }),
  ]);

  const events: TimelineEvent[] = [];

  const primaryVisits = (primaryVisitsRes.data ?? []) as {
    id: string;
    visited_at: string;
    amount: number;
  }[];

  const companionVisitIds = ((companionMembershipsRes.data ?? []) as { visit_id: string }[]).map(
    (m) => m.visit_id
  );

  let companionVisits: {
    id: string;
    visited_at: string;
    amount: number;
    primary_customer_id: string;
  }[] = [];
  let primaryNameById = new Map<string, string>();

  if (companionVisitIds.length > 0) {
    const { data: companionVisitRows } = await supabase
      .from("visits")
      .select("id, visited_at, amount, primary_customer_id")
      .in("id", companionVisitIds)
      .eq("invalidated", false);
    companionVisits = (companionVisitRows ?? []) as typeof companionVisits;

    const primaryIds = [...new Set(companionVisits.map((v) => v.primary_customer_id))];
    if (primaryIds.length > 0) {
      const { data: primaryCustomers } = await supabase
        .from("customers")
        .select("id, display_name")
        .in("id", primaryIds);
      primaryNameById = new Map((primaryCustomers ?? []).map((c) => [c.id, c.display_name]));
    }
  }

  // 莉｣陦ｨ閠・蜷御ｼｴ閠・←縺｡繧峨・遶句ｴ縺九↓髢｢繧上ｉ縺壹∵律譎る・↓荳ｦ縺ｹ縺ｦ譛蛻昴・1莉ｶ繧偵悟・蝗樊擂蠎励阪→縺吶ｋ
  type VisitOccurrence = { id: string; visited_at: string; amount: number; role: "primary" | "companion"; companionOfName: string | null };
  const allVisits: VisitOccurrence[] = [
    ...primaryVisits.map((v) => ({ ...v, role: "primary" as const, companionOfName: null })),
    ...companionVisits.map((v) => ({
      id: v.id,
      visited_at: v.visited_at,
      amount: v.amount,
      role: "companion" as const,
      companionOfName: primaryNameById.get(v.primary_customer_id) ?? null,
    })),
  ].sort((a, b) => (a.visited_at < b.visited_at ? -1 : 1));

  allVisits.forEach((v, i) => {
    const isFirst = i === 0;
    const roleNote = v.role === "companion" ? `莉｣陦ｨ閠・ｼ・{v.companionOfName ?? "荳肴・"}讒倥・蜷御ｼｴ` : null;
    events.push({
      id: `visit-${v.role}-${v.id}`,
      date: v.visited_at,
      kind: isFirst ? "first_visit" : "visit",
      title: isFirst ? "蛻晏屓譚･蠎・ : v.role === "companion" ? "譚･蠎暦ｼ亥酔莨ｴ・・ : "譚･蠎・,
      detail: roleNote ?? `ﾂ･${v.amount.toLocaleString("ja-JP")}`,
    });
  });

  for (const b of (bottlesRes.data ?? []) as {
    id: string;
    bottle_type: string | null;
    bottle_name: string;
    created_at: string;
  }[]) {
    events.push({
      id: `bottle-${b.id}`,
      date: b.created_at,
      kind: "bottle",
      title: "繝懊ヨ繝ｫ霑ｽ蜉",
      detail: b.bottle_type || b.bottle_name,
    });
  }

  const RESERVATION_STATUS_LABEL: Record<string, string> = {
    reserved: "莠育ｴ・,
    visited: "莠育ｴ・ｼ域擂蠎玲ｸ茨ｼ・,
    cancelled: "莠育ｴ・ｼ医く繝｣繝ｳ繧ｻ繝ｫ・・,
  };
  for (const r of (reservationsRes.data ?? []) as {
    id: string;
    reserved_at: string;
    status: string;
    created_at: string;
  }[]) {
    events.push({
      id: `reservation-${r.id}`,
      date: r.created_at,
      kind: "reservation",
      title: RESERVATION_STATUS_LABEL[r.status] ?? "莠育ｴ・,
      detail: `莠育ｴ・律譎ゑｼ・{r.reserved_at.slice(0, 16).replace("T", " ")}`,
    });
  }

  for (const n of (notesRes.data ?? []) as { id: string; note: string; created_at: string }[]) {
    events.push({
      id: `note-${n.id}`,
      date: n.created_at,
      kind: "note",
      title: "繝｡繝｢霑ｽ蜉",
      detail: n.note,
    });
  }

  for (const c of (champagnesRes.data ?? []) as { id: string; name: string; created_at: string }[]) {
    events.push({
      id: `champagne-${c.id}`,
      date: c.created_at,
      kind: "champagne",
      title: "繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ霑ｽ蜉",
      detail: c.name,
    });
  }

  return events.sort((a, b) => (a.date < b.date ? 1 : -1));
}



--- filename: \src\lib\data\visits.ts ---

import { createClient } from "@/lib/supabase/server";
import type { Customer, Visit, Tag, PaymentMethod, SeatType } from "@/types/database";
import { toErrorMessage } from "@/lib/error-message";

/**
 * 鬘ｧ螳｢蜷阪が繝ｼ繝医さ繝ｳ繝励Μ繝ｼ繝茨ｼ育ｬｬ5遶・峨・ * display_name / kana 縺ｮ蜑肴婿荳閾ｴ蟇・ｊ縺ｮ驛ｨ蛻・ｸ閾ｴ縺ｧ鬮倬溘↓蛟呵｣懊ｒ霑斐☆縲・ * trigram繧､繝ｳ繝・ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ・・03・峨ｒ蛻ｩ逕ｨ縺吶ｋ縺溘ａ500莉ｶ隕乗ｨ｡縺ｧ繧ょ香蛻・ｫ倬溘・ */
export async function searchCustomerNames(
  query: string,
  limit = 8
): Promise<Pick<Customer, "id" | "display_name" | "kana" | "caution_level">[]> {
  if (!query.trim()) return [];
  const supabase = await createClient();
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from("customers")
    .select("id, display_name, kana, caution_level")
    .eq("hidden", false)
    .or(`display_name.ilike.%${query}%,kana.ilike.%${query}%`)
    .limit(limit);
  if (error) throw error;
  return data ?? [];
}

export type LastVisitInfo = {
  seat_type: SeatType | null;
  payment_method: PaymentMethod;
  receipt_required: boolean;
  receipt_name: string | null;
  tags: Tag[];
  companionNames: string[];
  memo: string | null;
  hasHistory: boolean;
};

/**
 * 譌｢蟄倬｡ｧ螳｢縺ｮ縲梧擂蠎励阪・繧ｿ繝ｳ縺九ｉ髢九＞縺溷ｴ蜷医・蜑榊屓諠・ｱ閾ｪ蜍募・蜉幢ｼ育ｬｬ4遶繝ｻ隨ｬ5遶繝ｻ隨ｬ19遶・峨・ * 蜑榊屓繧ｿ繧ｰ繝ｻ蜑榊屓鬆伜庶譖ｸ螳帛錐繝ｻ蜑榊屓蜷御ｼｴ閠・・蜑榊屓繝｡繝｢繧貞叙蠕励☆繧九・ * 莨夊ｨ磯≡鬘阪・繝√ャ繝励・豈主屓螟峨ｏ繧九◆繧∝ｼ輔″邯吶′縺ｪ縺・ｼ医Ξ繝薙Η繝ｼ謖・遭・壼燕蝗樊擂蠎励さ繝斐・・峨・ *
 * RC8菫ｮ豁｣: 莉｣陦ｨ閠・→縺励※縺ｮ譚･蠎励□縺代〒縺ｪ縺上∝酔莨ｴ閠・→縺励※譚･蠎励＠縺溷ｱ･豁ｴ繧・ * 縲悟燕蝗樊擂蠎励阪・蛟呵｣懊↓蜷ｫ繧√ｋ・医←縺｡繧峨・遶句ｴ縺ｧ繧ゅ√ｈ繧頑眠縺励＞譁ｹ繧呈治逕ｨ縺吶ｋ・峨・ * 繝懊ヨ繝ｫ縺ｯ譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ縺九ｉ蛻・ｊ髮｢縺励◆縺溘ａ縲√％縺薙〒縺ｯ謇ｱ繧上↑縺・・ */
export async function getLastVisitInfo(
  customerId: string
): Promise<LastVisitInfo | null> {
  const supabase = await createClient();

  const [primaryVisitRes, companionVisitRes, tagsRes] = await Promise.all([
    supabase
      .from("visits")
      .select("*")
      .eq("primary_customer_id", customerId)
      .eq("invalidated", false)
      .order("visited_at", { ascending: false })
      .limit(1)
      .maybeSingle(),
    supabase
      .from("visit_members")
      .select("visits(*)")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId)
      .eq("member_type", "companion")
      .order("created_at", { ascending: false })
      .limit(5),
    supabase
      .from("customer_tags")
      .select("tags(*)")
      .eq("customer_id", customerId),
  ]);

  const primaryVisit = primaryVisitRes.data as Visit | null;

  // 蜷御ｼｴ閠・→縺励※縺ｮ譚･蠎怜呵｣懊°繧峨∫┌蜉ｹ蛹悶＆繧後※縺・↑縺・ｂ縺ｮ縺ｮ縺・■譛譁ｰ縺ｮ1莉ｶ繧帝∈縺ｶ
  const companionVisitCandidates = (
    (companionVisitRes.data ?? []) as unknown as { visits: Visit | null }[]
  )
    .map((row) => row.visits)
    .filter((v): v is Visit => !!v && !v.invalidated)
    .sort((a, b) => (a.visited_at < b.visited_at ? 1 : -1));
  const companionVisit = companionVisitCandidates[0] ?? null;

  // 莉｣陦ｨ閠・→縺励※縺ｮ譚･蠎励・蜷御ｼｴ閠・→縺励※縺ｮ譚･蠎励・縺・■縲√ｈ繧頑眠縺励＞譁ｹ繧偵悟燕蝗樊擂蠎励阪→縺励※謗｡逕ｨ縺吶ｋ
  const lastVisit =
    !primaryVisit && !companionVisit
      ? null
      : !primaryVisit
      ? companionVisit
      : !companionVisit
      ? primaryVisit
      : primaryVisit.visited_at >= companionVisit.visited_at
      ? primaryVisit
      : companionVisit;

  const tags = ((tagsRes.data ?? []) as unknown as { tags: Tag }[])
    .map((r) => r.tags)
    .filter(Boolean);

  let companionNames: string[] = [];
  if (lastVisit) {
    const { data: memberRows } = await supabase
      .from("visit_members")
      .select("customer_id")
      .eq("visit_id", lastVisit.id)
      .eq("member_type", "companion");
    const cIds = (memberRows ?? []).map((m: { customer_id: string }) => m.customer_id);
    if (cIds.length > 0) {
      const { data: cData } = await supabase
        .from("customers")
        .select("id, display_name")
        .in("id", cIds);
      companionNames = (cData ?? []).map((c: { display_name: string }) => c.display_name);
    }
  }

  return {
    seat_type: lastVisit?.seat_type ?? null,
    payment_method: lastVisit?.payment_method ?? "cash",
    receipt_required: lastVisit?.receipt_required ?? false,
    receipt_name: lastVisit?.receipt_name ?? null,
    tags,
    companionNames,
    memo: lastVisit?.memo ?? null,
    hasHistory: !!lastVisit,
  };
}

export type NewVisitInput = {
  customerId: string;
  isNewCustomer: boolean;
  newCustomerName?: string;
  newCustomerKana?: string;
  newCustomerBirthday?: string;
  visitedAt: string; // ISO譁・ｭ怜・
  peopleCount: number;
  companionNames: string[]; // 譛螟ｧ10蜷搾ｼ育ｬｬ4遶・・  companionKanas: string[]; // companionNames縺ｨ蜷後§荳ｦ縺ｳ鬆・ｼ医Ξ繝薙Η繝ｼ謖・遭竭ｨ・・  companionBirthdays: string[]; // 譛・譌･縺ｮ縺ｿ (2000-MM-DD 蠖｢蠑・ 譛ｪ蜈･蜉帙・遨ｺ譁・ｭ・
  amount: number;
  tip: number;
  paymentMethod: PaymentMethod;
  seatType: SeatType | null;
  receiptRequired: boolean;
  receiptName: string | null;
  tagIds: string[];
  memo: string | null;
  /** 莠育ｴ・°繧峨・蠑輔″邯吶℃縺ｮ蝣ｴ蜷医∵擂蠎礼匳骭ｲ螳御ｺ・→蜷梧凾縺ｫ莠育ｴ・ｒ縲梧擂蠎玲ｸ医阪↓縺吶ｋ・育ｬｬ10遶・・*/
  reservationId?: string | null;
};

/**
 * 譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ縺ｮ菫晏ｭ假ｼ育ｬｬ4遶繝ｻ隨ｬ18遶繝ｻ隨ｬ30遶・峨・ *
 * RC8菫ｮ豁｣: 菫晏ｭ伜ｮ牙ｮ壽ｧ繧呈怙蜆ｪ蜈医☆繧九◆繧√√・繝医Ν繝ｻ繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ縺ｮ菫晏ｭ倥ｒ
 * 譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ縺ｮ菫晏ｭ伜・逅・°繧牙ｮ悟・縺ｫ蛻・ｊ髮｢縺励◆縲ゅ・繝医Ν縺ｯ鬘ｧ螳｢隧ｳ邏ｰ縺ｮ
 * 縲後・繝医Ν霑ｽ蜉縲阪°繧峨・縺ｿ逋ｻ骭ｲ縺吶ｋ・亥ｾ捺擂縺九ｉ螳牙ｮ壹＠縺ｦ蜍穂ｽ懊＠縺ｦ縺・ｋ邨瑚ｷｯ・峨・ * 縺薙ｌ縺ｫ繧医ｊ譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ縺ｮ菫晏ｭ伜・逅・・縲碁｡ｧ螳｢繝ｻ譚･蠎励・蜷御ｼｴ閠・・繧ｿ繧ｰ繝ｻ莠育ｴ・峩譁ｰ縲阪・
 * 1繝医Λ繝ｳ繧ｶ繧ｯ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ縺ｮ縺ｿ縺ｨ縺ｪ繧翫∝､ｱ謨苓ｦ∝屏繧貞､ｧ蟷・↓貂帙ｉ縺励※縺・ｋ縲・ */
export async function createVisit(input: NewVisitInput) {
  const supabase = await createClient();

  const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc("create_visit_with_details", {
    p_customer_id: input.isNewCustomer ? null : input.customerId,
    p_is_new_customer: input.isNewCustomer,
    p_new_customer_name: input.newCustomerName ?? null,
    p_visited_at: input.visitedAt,
    p_people_count: input.peopleCount,
    p_companion_names: input.companionNames,
    p_amount: input.amount,
    p_tip: input.tip,
    p_payment_method: input.paymentMethod,
    p_seat_type: input.seatType,
    p_receipt_required: input.receiptRequired,
    p_receipt_name: input.receiptName,
    p_memo: input.memo,
    p_tag_ids: input.tagIds,
    p_reservation_id: input.reservationId ?? null,
    p_new_customer_kana: input.newCustomerKana ?? null,
    p_new_customer_birthday: input.newCustomerBirthday || null,
    p_companion_kanas: input.companionKanas,
    p_companion_birthdays: input.companionBirthdays,
  });

  if (error) {
    throw new Error(toErrorMessage(error, "菫晏ｭ倥〒縺阪∪縺帙ｓ縺ｧ縺励◆縲ゅｂ縺・ｸ蠎ｦ縺願ｩｦ縺励￥縺縺輔＞縲・));
  }

  const result = data as unknown as { visit_id?: string; customer_id?: string };

  if (!result?.customer_id || !result?.visit_id) {
    throw new Error(
      "譚･蠎励・菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ縺ｫID縺ｮ蜿門ｾ励↓螟ｱ謨励＠縺ｾ縺励◆縲ゅｂ縺・ｸ蠎ｦ縺願ｩｦ縺励￥縺縺輔＞・域隼蝟・＠縺ｪ縺・ｴ蜷医・縺秘｣邨｡縺上□縺輔＞・峨・
    );
  }

  return { visitId: result.visit_id, customerId: result.customer_id };
}



--- filename: \src\lib\offline\customer-cache.ts ---

import {
  dbReplaceCustomerCache,
  dbGetAllCachedCustomers,
  dbGetCustomerCacheCount,
  dbSetMeta,
  dbGetMeta,
  type CachedCustomer,
} from "./db";
import { fetchCustomerCacheAction } from "@/lib/actions/customer-cache";

const LAST_SYNCED_KEY = "customer-cache-last-synced-at";

export type CacheStatus = {
  syncing: boolean;
  count: number;
  lastSyncedAt: string | null;
};

type Listener = (status: CacheStatus) => void;
const listeners = new Set<Listener>();
let currentStatus: CacheStatus = { syncing: false, count: 0, lastSyncedAt: null };
let syncInFlight = false;

function emit() {
  listeners.forEach((l) => l(currentStatus));
}

export function subscribeCacheStatus(listener: Listener): () => void {
  listeners.add(listener);
  listener(currentStatus);
  // 蛻晏屓雉ｼ隱ｭ譎ゅ↓菫晏ｭ俶ｸ医∩縺ｮ莉ｶ謨ｰ繝ｻ蜷梧悄譎ょ綾繧定ｪｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ繧
  void (async () => {
    try {
      const [count, lastSyncedAt] = await Promise.all([
        dbGetCustomerCacheCount(),
        dbGetMeta(LAST_SYNCED_KEY),
      ]);
      currentStatus = { ...currentStatus, count, lastSyncedAt };
      emit();
    } catch {
      // IndexedDB譛ｪ蟇ｾ蠢懃腸蠅・〒縺ｯ辟｡隕悶☆繧・    }
  })();
  return () => listeners.delete(listener);
}

function buildSearchBlob(input: {
  display_name: string;
  kana: string | null;
  real_name: string | null;
  memo: string | null;
  aliases: string[];
  tags: string[];
  receiptNames: string[];
}): string {
  return [
    input.display_name,
    input.kana ?? "",
    input.real_name ?? "",
    input.memo ?? "",
    ...input.aliases,
    ...input.tags,
    ...input.receiptNames,
  ]
    .join(" ")
    .toLowerCase();
}

/**
 * 繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・縺九ｉ譛譁ｰ1000莉ｶ・育ｬｬ38遶縺ｮ隕∽ｻｶ・峨ｒ蜿門ｾ励＠縲！ndexedDB繧剃ｸｸ縺斐→蜈･繧梧崛縺医ｋ縲・ * 繧ｪ繝ｳ繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ譎・ 襍ｷ蜍墓凾繝ｻ繧ｪ繝ｳ繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ蠕ｩ蟶ｰ譎ゅ・5蛻・＃縺ｨ縺ｮ繝舌ャ繧ｯ繧ｰ繝ｩ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝画峩譁ｰ縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｰ繧後ｋ縲・ */
export async function syncCustomerCache(): Promise<void> {
  if (syncInFlight) return;
  if (typeof navigator !== "undefined" && !navigator.onLine) return;

  syncInFlight = true;
  currentStatus = { ...currentStatus, syncing: true };
  emit();

  try {
    const records = await fetchCustomerCacheAction();
    const cached: CachedCustomer[] = records.map((r) => ({
      ...r,
      searchBlob: buildSearchBlob(r),
    }));
    await dbReplaceCustomerCache(cached);
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    await dbSetMeta(LAST_SYNCED_KEY, now);
    currentStatus = { syncing: false, count: cached.length, lastSyncedAt: now };
  } catch {
    // 繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ繝ｻ騾壻ｿ｡繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ譎ゅ・譌｢蟄倥く繝｣繝・す繝･繧偵◎縺ｮ縺ｾ縺ｾ邯ｭ謖√☆繧・    currentStatus = { ...currentStatus, syncing: false };
  } finally {
    syncInFlight = false;
    emit();
  }
}

export type SearchResult = {
  id: string;
  display_name: string;
  kana: string | null;
  real_name: string | null;
  favorite: boolean;
  rank: string;
  last_visit_at: string | null;
  visit_count: number;
  tags: string[];
};

/** 繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ讀懃ｴ｢・育ｬｬ9遶繝ｻ隨ｬ19遶・壼錐蜑阪・縺ｵ繧翫′縺ｪ繝ｻ譛ｬ蜷阪・繧ｿ繧ｰ繝ｻ鬆伜庶譖ｸ螳帛錐繝ｻ繝｡繝｢縺悟ｯｾ雎｡・峨・*/
export async function searchCachedCustomers(query: string): Promise<SearchResult[]> {
  const term = query.trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!term) return [];

  const all = await dbGetAllCachedCustomers();
  return all
    .filter((c) => c.searchBlob.includes(term))
    .sort((a, b) => (b.last_visit_at ?? "").localeCompare(a.last_visit_at ?? ""))
    .slice(0, 50)
    .map((c) => ({
      id: c.id,
      display_name: c.display_name,
      kana: c.kana,
      real_name: c.real_name,
      favorite: c.favorite,
      rank: c.rank,
      last_visit_at: c.last_visit_at,
      visit_count: c.visit_count,
      tags: c.tags,
    }));
}



--- filename: \src\lib\offline\db.ts ---

const DB_NAME = "both151a-offline";
const DB_VERSION = 2;
const STORE = "pending-writes";
const CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE = "customer-cache";
const META_STORE = "meta";

export type PendingWriteKind = "visit" | "reservation" | "note";

export type PendingWrite = {
  id: string;
  kind: PendingWriteKind;
  /** FormData縺ｯ逶ｴ謗･菫晏ｭ倥〒縺阪↑縺・◆繧・[key, value] 縺ｮ繧ｿ繝励Ν蛻励↓螟画鋤縺励※菫晏ｭ倥☆繧・*/
  entries: [string, string][];
  createdAt: string;
};

function openDb(): Promise<IDBDatabase> {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const req = indexedDB.open(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
    req.onupgradeneeded = () => {
      const db = req.result;
      if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE)) {
        db.createObjectStore(STORE, { keyPath: "id" });
      }
      if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE)) {
        const store = db.createObjectStore(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE, { keyPath: "id" });
        // last_visit_at 縺ｮ譁ｰ縺励＞鬆・↓蜿悶ｊ蜃ｺ縺帙ｋ繧医≧縺ｫ縺吶ｋ・・000莉ｶ蜆ｪ蜈亥ｺｦ縺ｮ遒ｺ隱阪・謨ｴ逅・↓菴ｿ縺・ｼ・        store.createIndex("last_visit_at", "last_visit_at");
      }
      if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(META_STORE)) {
        db.createObjectStore(META_STORE, { keyPath: "key" });
      }
    };
    req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result);
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}

export function formDataToEntries(formData: FormData): [string, string][] {
  return Array.from(formData.entries()).map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)]);
}

export function entriesToFormData(entries: [string, string][]): FormData {
  const fd = new FormData();
  for (const [k, v] of entries) fd.append(k, v);
  return fd;
}

export async function dbAddPendingWrite(write: PendingWrite): Promise<void> {
  const db = await openDb();
  await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(STORE, "readwrite");
    tx.objectStore(STORE).put(write);
    tx.oncomplete = () => resolve();
    tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error);
  });
}

export async function dbListPendingWrites(): Promise<PendingWrite[]> {
  const db = await openDb();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(STORE, "readonly");
    const req = tx.objectStore(STORE).getAll();
    req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result as PendingWrite[]);
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}

export async function dbRemovePendingWrite(id: string): Promise<void> {
  const db = await openDb();
  await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(STORE, "readwrite");
    tx.objectStore(STORE).delete(id);
    tx.oncomplete = () => resolve();
    tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error);
  });
}

// ============================================================
// 鬘ｧ螳｢讀懃ｴ｢繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･・医が繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ讀懃ｴ｢逕ｨ繝ｻ隨ｬ9遶繝ｻ隨ｬ19遶繝ｻ隨ｬ38遶・・// ============================================================

export type CachedCustomer = {
  id: string;
  display_name: string;
  kana: string | null;
  real_name: string | null;
  memo: string | null;
  favorite: boolean;
  rank: string;
  last_visit_at: string | null;
  visit_count: number;
  aliases: string[];
  tags: string[];
  receiptNames: string[];
  /** 讀懃ｴ｢逕ｨ縺ｫ蟆乗枚蟄怜喧繝ｻ邨仙粋貂医∩縺ｮ譁・ｭ怜・・域ｯ主屓邨仙粋縺励↑縺・ｈ縺・ｺ句燕險育ｮ励＠縺ｦ縺翫￥・・*/
  searchBlob: string;
};

/** 繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･蜈ｨ莉ｶ繧堤ｽｮ縺肴鋤縺医ｋ・亥酔譛溘・縺溘・縺ｫ譛譁ｰ1000莉ｶ縺ｧ荳ｸ縺斐→蜈･繧梧崛縺医ｋ・峨・*/
export async function dbReplaceCustomerCache(records: CachedCustomer[]): Promise<void> {
  const db = await openDb();
  await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE, "readwrite");
    const store = tx.objectStore(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE);
    store.clear();
    for (const record of records) store.put(record);
    tx.oncomplete = () => resolve();
    tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error);
  });
}

export async function dbGetAllCachedCustomers(): Promise<CachedCustomer[]> {
  const db = await openDb();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE, "readonly");
    const req = tx.objectStore(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE).getAll();
    req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result as CachedCustomer[]);
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}

export async function dbGetCustomerCacheCount(): Promise<number> {
  const db = await openDb();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE, "readonly");
    const req = tx.objectStore(CUSTOMER_CACHE_STORE).count();
    req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result);
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}

export async function dbSetMeta(key: string, value: string): Promise<void> {
  const db = await openDb();
  await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(META_STORE, "readwrite");
    tx.objectStore(META_STORE).put({ key, value });
    tx.oncomplete = () => resolve();
    tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error);
  });
}

export async function dbGetMeta(key: string): Promise<string | null> {
  const db = await openDb();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const tx = db.transaction(META_STORE, "readonly");
    const req = tx.objectStore(META_STORE).get(key);
    req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result ? (req.result.value as string) : null);
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}



--- filename: \src\lib\offline\queue.ts ---

import {
  dbAddPendingWrite,
  dbListPendingWrites,
  dbRemovePendingWrite,
  formDataToEntries,
  entriesToFormData,
  type PendingWriteKind,
} from "./db";

type Listener = (count: number) => void;
const listeners = new Set<Listener>();

async function notifyListeners() {
  try {
    const count = (await dbListPendingWrites()).length;
    listeners.forEach((l) => l(count));
  } catch {
    // IndexedDB譛ｪ蟇ｾ蠢懃腸蠅・↑縺ｩ縺ｧ縺ｯ騾夂衍繧偵せ繧ｭ繝・・縺吶ｋ
  }
}

/** 菫晉蕗荳ｭ縺ｮ譖ｸ縺崎ｾｼ縺ｿ莉ｶ謨ｰ縺ｮ螟牙喧繧定ｳｼ隱ｭ縺吶ｋ・医が繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ繝舌リ繝ｼ陦ｨ遉ｺ逕ｨ・峨・*/
export function subscribePendingCount(listener: Listener): () => void {
  listeners.add(listener);
  void notifyListeners();
  return () => {
    listeners.delete(listener);
  };
}

/**
 * 騾壻ｿ｡譁ｭ譎ゅ↓譖ｸ縺崎ｾｼ縺ｿ繧堤ｫｯ譛ｫ縺ｸ荳譎ゆｿ晏ｭ倥☆繧具ｼ育ｬｬ38遶・峨・ * 騾壻ｿ｡蠕ｩ譌ｧ蠕後’lushQueue() 縺ｧ閾ｪ蜍慕噪縺ｫSupabase縺ｸ蜷梧悄縺輔ｌ繧九・ */
export async function enqueueWrite(kind: PendingWriteKind, formData: FormData): Promise<void> {
  await dbAddPendingWrite({
    id: `${kind}-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`,
    kind,
    entries: formDataToEntries(formData),
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });
  await notifyListeners();
}

export async function getPendingCount(): Promise<number> {
  try {
    return (await dbListPendingWrites()).length;
  } catch {
    return 0;
  }
}

type Handlers = Record<PendingWriteKind, (formData: FormData) => Promise<unknown>>;

/**
 * 菫晉蕗荳ｭ縺ｮ譖ｸ縺崎ｾｼ縺ｿ繧帝・分縺ｫ蜀埼∽ｿ｡縺吶ｋ縲・ * 螟ｱ謨励＠縺滓凾轤ｹ縺ｧ蛛懈ｭ｢縺吶ｋ・医∪縺騾壻ｿ｡縺御ｸ榊ｮ牙ｮ壹↑蜿ｯ閭ｽ諤ｧ縺後≠繧九◆繧√∵ｬ｡蝗槭が繝ｳ繝ｩ繧､繝ｳ蠕ｩ蟶ｰ譎ゅ↓蜀崎ｩｦ陦鯉ｼ峨・ * 隨ｬ38遶縲檎ｫｶ蜷医′逋ｺ逕溘＠縺溷ｴ蜷医・譛蠕後↓菫晏ｭ倥＆繧後◆蜀・ｮｹ繧呈治逕ｨ縺励∫屮譟ｻ繝ｭ繧ｰ縺ｫ荳｡譁ｹ縺ｮ螟画峩繧呈ｮ九☆縲阪・
 * DB蛛ｴ縺ｮ逶｣譟ｻ繝ｭ繧ｰ繝医Μ繧ｬ繝ｼ・・04・峨′蜷・嶌縺崎ｾｼ縺ｿ繧貞句挨縺ｫ險倬鹸縺吶ｋ縺薙→縺ｧ諡・ｿ昴☆繧九・ */
export async function flushQueue(handlers: Handlers): Promise<number> {
  let synced = 0;
  try {
    const items = await dbListPendingWrites();
    // 逋ｻ骭ｲ縺輔ｌ縺滄・↓蜷梧悄縺吶ｋ
    items.sort((a, b) => a.createdAt.localeCompare(b.createdAt));

    for (const item of items) {
      try {
        await handlers[item.kind](entriesToFormData(item.entries));
        await dbRemovePendingWrite(item.id);
        synced++;
      } catch {
        break; // 縺ｾ縺騾∽ｿ｡縺ｧ縺阪↑縺・ｴ蜷医・縺薙％縺ｧ謇薙■蛻・ｊ縲∵ｬ｡蝗槭・蜷梧悄繧ｿ繧､繝溘Φ繧ｰ縺ｫ莉ｻ縺帙ｋ
      }
    }
  } catch {
    // IndexedDB譛ｪ蟇ｾ蠢懃腸蠅・〒縺ｯ菴輔ｂ縺励↑縺・  } finally {
    await notifyListeners();
  }
  return synced;
}



--- filename: \src\lib\offline\useOnlineStatus.ts ---

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";

/**
 * 騾壻ｿ｡迥ｶ諷九ｒ逶｣隕悶☆繧九ヵ繝・け・育ｬｬ38遶縲後が繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ菫晏ｭ倅ｸｭ縲崎｡ｨ遉ｺ縺ｮ蛻､螳壹↓菴ｿ逕ｨ・峨・ *
 * RC3菫ｮ豁｣: 蛻晄悄蛟､縺ｧ navigator.onLine 繧堤峩謗･隱ｭ繧縺ｨ縲√し繝ｼ繝舌・謠冗判・亥ｸｸ縺ｫtrue謇ｱ縺・ｼ峨→
 * 繧ｯ繝ｩ繧､繧｢繝ｳ繝亥・蝗樊緒逕ｻ縺ｮ邨先棡縺御ｸ閾ｴ縺励↑縺・ｴ蜷医↓ Hydration Error 繧定ｵｷ縺薙＠縺・ｋ
 * ・育音縺ｫ荳驛ｨ縺ｮAndroid繧ｿ繝悶Ξ繝・ヨ縺ｧ縺ｯnavigator.onLine縺御ｸ榊ｮ牙ｮ壹↓ false 繧定ｿ斐☆縺薙→縺後≠繧具ｼ峨・ * 縺薙・繝輔ャ繧ｯ縺ｯ AppShell 邨檎罰縺ｧ蜈ｨ繝壹・繧ｸ縺ｫ蟶ｸ譎ゅ・繧ｦ繝ｳ繝医＆繧後ｋ縺溘ａ縲√％縺薙〒縺ｮ
 * Hydration Error縺ｯ繧｢繝励Μ蜈ｨ菴薙・繧､繝吶Φ繝医ワ繝ｳ繝峨Λ蝟ｪ螟ｱ縺ｫ豕｢蜿翫＠縺・ｋ縲・ * 縺昴・縺溘ａ蛻晄悄蛟､縺ｯ蟶ｸ縺ｫ繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・縺ｨ蜷後§ true 縺ｨ縺励∝ｮ滄圀縺ｮ迥ｶ諷九・繝槭え繝ｳ繝亥ｾ後↓陬懈ｭ｣縺吶ｋ縲・ */
export function useOnlineStatus(): boolean {
  const [online, setOnline] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    // 繝槭え繝ｳ繝亥ｾ鯉ｼ医ワ繧､繝峨Ξ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ螳御ｺ・ｾ鯉ｼ峨↓螳滄圀縺ｮ迥ｶ諷九∈陬懈ｭ｣縺吶ｋ
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/set-state-in-effect -- 螟夜ΚAPI(navigator.onLine)縺ｸ縺ｮ蜷梧悄縺ｮ縺溘ａ諢丞峙逧・    setOnline(typeof navigator === "undefined" ? true : navigator.onLine);

    const handleOnline = () => setOnline(true);
    const handleOffline = () => setOnline(false);
    window.addEventListener("online", handleOnline);
    window.addEventListener("offline", handleOffline);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener("online", handleOnline);
      window.removeEventListener("offline", handleOffline);
    };
  }, []);

  return online;
}



--- filename: \src\lib\supabase\middleware.ts ---

import { createServerClient } from "@supabase/ssr";
import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";

// 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ荳崎ｦ√〒繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ縺ｧ縺阪ｋ繝代せ・育ｬｬ41遶: 譛ｪ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ迥ｶ諷九〒縺ｯ荳蛻・・逕ｻ髱｢繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺励↑縺・縺ｮ蜚ｯ荳縺ｮ萓句､厄ｼ・const PUBLIC_PATHS = ["/login"];

function isPublicPath(pathname: string) {
  return (
    PUBLIC_PATHS.some((p) => pathname === p || pathname.startsWith(p + "/")) ||
    pathname.startsWith("/_next") ||
    pathname.startsWith("/manifest") ||
    pathname.startsWith("/icons") ||
    pathname === "/favicon.ico" ||
    pathname === "/offline.html" ||
    pathname === "/sw.js"
  );
}

/**
 * 蜈ｨ繝ｪ繧ｯ繧ｨ繧ｹ繝医〒Supabase繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ繧呈､懆ｨｼ繝ｻ繝ｪ繝輔Ξ繝・す繝･縺励・ * 譛ｪ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ繧偵Ο繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ逕ｻ髱｢縺ｸ繝ｪ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝医☆繧九・ *
 * v1.2菫ｮ豁｣:
 * 繝ｻ繧ｿ繝悶Ξ繝・ヨ縺ｧ縺ｮ繝壹・繧ｸ驕ｷ遘ｻ蠕後↓繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ逕ｻ髱｢縺ｸ謌ｻ繧句撫鬘後ｒ菫ｮ豁｣
 * 繝ｻ繧ｿ繧､繝繧｢繧ｦ繝医ｒ10遘偵↓蟒ｶ髟ｷ縺励∽ｸ譎ら噪縺ｪ謗･邯壽妙縺ｧ縺ｮ隱､繝ｪ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝医ｒ髦ｲ豁｢
 * 繝ｻ繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳCookie縺悟ｭ伜惠縺吶ｋ蝣ｴ蜷医・繧ｿ繧､繝繧｢繧ｦ繝医〒繧ゅΜ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝医＠縺ｪ縺・ * 繝ｻgetSession()縺ｧCookie縺九ｉ繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ隱ｭ縺ｿ蜿悶ｊ縲“etUser()縺ｧ繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・讀懆ｨｼ縺ｮ2谿ｵ髫弱↓螟画峩
 */
export async function updateSession(request: NextRequest) {
  let supabaseResponse = NextResponse.next({ request });

  const supabase = createServerClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        getAll() {
          return request.cookies.getAll();
        },
        setAll(cookiesToSet) {
          cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value }) =>
            request.cookies.set(name, value)
          );
          supabaseResponse = NextResponse.next({ request });
          cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>
            supabaseResponse.cookies.set(name, value, options)
          );
        },
      },
      global: {
        fetch: (input, init) =>
          fetch(input, { ...init, cache: "no-store", signal: AbortSignal.timeout(10000) }),
      },
    }
  );

  const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;

  // Cookie縺ｫ繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ縺後≠繧九°縺ｩ縺・°繧偵∪縺夂｢ｺ隱搾ｼ医ロ繝・ヨ繝ｯ繝ｼ繧ｯ荳崎ｦ・ｼ・  const { data: sessionData } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
  const hasSessionCookie = !!sessionData?.session;

  let user = null;
  let authError = false;
  try {
    const { data } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    user = data.user;
  } catch {
    // 繧ｿ繧､繝繧｢繧ｦ繝医・繝阪ャ繝医Ρ繝ｼ繧ｯ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ譎・    authError = true;
    // Cookie縺ｫ繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ縺悟ｭ伜惠縺吶ｋ蝣ｴ蜷医・繝ｪ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝医＠縺ｪ縺・    // 竊・繧ｿ繝悶Ξ繝・ヨ縺ｧ縺ｮ繝壹・繧ｸ驕ｷ遘ｻ蠕後↓繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ逕ｻ髱｢縺ｫ鬟帙・蝠城｡後・荳ｻ蝗
    if (hasSessionCookie) {
      return supabaseResponse;
    }
    user = null;
  }

  // 繝阪ャ繝医Ρ繝ｼ繧ｯ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺ｧCookie繧ゅ↑縺・ｴ蜷医・縺ｿ繝ｪ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝・  if (!user && !authError && !isPublicPath(pathname)) {
    const loginUrl = new URL("/login", request.url);
    loginUrl.searchParams.set("redirectedFrom", pathname);
    return NextResponse.redirect(loginUrl);
  }

  if (!user && authError && !hasSessionCookie && !isPublicPath(pathname)) {
    const loginUrl = new URL("/login", request.url);
    loginUrl.searchParams.set("redirectedFrom", pathname);
    return NextResponse.redirect(loginUrl);
  }

  if (user && pathname === "/login") {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/dashboard", request.url));
  }

  return supabaseResponse;
}



--- filename: \src\lib\supabase\server.ts ---

import { createServerClient } from "@supabase/ssr";
import { cookies } from "next/headers";
import type { Database } from "@/types/database";

/**
 * 繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・繧ｳ繝ｳ繝昴・繝阪Φ繝・/ Server Action / Route Handler 縺九ｉ蛻ｩ逕ｨ縺吶ｋSupabase繧ｯ繝ｩ繧､繧｢繝ｳ繝医・ * Cookie繝吶・繧ｹ縺ｧ繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ繧定ｪｭ縺ｿ譖ｸ縺阪☆繧九・ */
export async function createClient() {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();

  return createServerClient<Database>(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        getAll() {
          return cookieStore.getAll();
        },
        setAll(cookiesToSet) {
          try {
            cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>
              cookieStore.set(name, value, options)
            );
          } catch {
            // Server Component 縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｰ繧後◆蝣ｴ蜷医・Cookie譖ｸ縺崎ｾｼ縺ｿ縺後〒縺阪↑縺・◆繧∫┌隕悶☆繧九・            // 繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ縺ｮ繝ｪ繝輔Ξ繝・す繝･縺ｯ middleware.ts 蛛ｴ縺ｧ陦後ｏ繧後ｋ縲・          }
        },
      },
      global: {
        // Supabase譛ｪ險ｭ螳壹・騾壻ｿ｡譁ｭ譎ゅ↓辟｡髯仙ｾ・ｩ溘＠縺ｪ縺・◆繧√・繧ｿ繧､繝繧｢繧ｦ繝茨ｼ磯壻ｿ｡繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ蟇ｾ遲厄ｼ・        // + v1.1菫ｮ豁｣: 譛ｬ逡ｪ迺ｰ蠅・〒Supabase縺ｮ蠢懃ｭ斐′繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･縺輔ｌ縲∵擂蠎礼匳骭ｲ逶ｴ蠕後・
        // 髮・ｨ医ｄ繧ｫ繝ｬ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺梧峩譁ｰ縺輔ｌ縺ｪ縺・ｸ榊・蜷医′縺ゅ▲縺溘◆繧√∵・遉ｺ逧・↓繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･辟｡蜉ｹ蛹悶☆繧九・        fetch: (input, init) =>
          fetch(input, { ...init, cache: "no-store", signal: AbortSignal.timeout(8000) }),
      },
    }
  );
}



--- filename: \src\lib\supabase\validate-env.ts ---

/**
 * Supabase URL險ｭ螳壹・邁｡譏薙ヰ繝ｪ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ縲・ * 繧医￥縺ゅｋ險ｭ螳壹Α繧ｹ縲袈RL縺ｮ譛ｫ蟆ｾ縺ｫ /rest/v1 繧貞性繧√※縺励∪縺・阪ｒ讀懃衍縺励・ * 蛻・°繧翫ｄ縺吶＞繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繝｡繝・そ繝ｼ繧ｸ繧定ｿ斐☆・・C2繝ｬ繝薙Η繝ｼ謖・遭蟇ｾ蠢懶ｼ峨・ */
export function validateSupabaseUrl(): string | null {
  const url = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL ?? "";

  if (!url) {
    return "迺ｰ蠅・､画焚 NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL 縺瑚ｨｭ螳壹＆繧後※縺・∪縺帙ｓ縲・env.local 繧堤｢ｺ隱阪＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・;
  }
  if (url.includes("/rest/v1")) {
    return "Supabase URL縺ｮ譛ｫ蟆ｾ縺ｫ /rest/v1 縺悟性縺ｾ繧後※縺・∪縺吶・env.local 縺ｮ NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL 縺ｯ縲敬ttps://xxxxx.supabase.co縲阪・蠖｢蠑擾ｼ・rest/v1 縺ｯ荳崎ｦ・ｼ峨↓縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲・;
  }
  if (!/^https:\/\/[a-z0-9-]+\.supabase\.co\/?$/.test(url) && !url.includes("dummy")) {
    // 繝繝溘・蛟､繧・峡閾ｪ繝峨Γ繧､繝ｳ驕狗畑縺ｪ縺ｩ豁｣蠖薙↑繧ｱ繝ｼ繧ｹ繧ゅ≠繧九◆繧√∬ｭｦ蜻翫・縺ｿ縺ｧ蜃ｦ逅・・豁｢繧√↑縺・    return null;
  }
  return null;
}



--- filename: \src\lib\bottle-expiry.ts ---

export type ExpiryTier = "expired" | "within7" | "within14" | "within30" | "safe";

/** 譛滄剞譌･縺九ｉ莉頑律縺ｾ縺ｧ縺ｮ譌･謨ｰ・郁ｲ謨ｰ=譛滄剞蛻・ｌ邨碁℃譌･謨ｰ・峨ｒ霑斐☆縲・*/
export function daysUntilExpiry(expiryDate: string): number {
  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const expiry = new Date(expiryDate);
  expiry.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  return Math.round((expiry.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
}

/**
 * 譛滄剞縺ｾ縺ｧ縺ｮ譌･謨ｰ縺九ｉ濶ｲ蛻・￠蛹ｺ蛻・ｒ蛻､螳壹☆繧具ｼ・谿ｵ髫弱・謗剃ｻ也噪・峨・ * 泙31譌･莉･荳・/ 泛30譌･莉･蜀・/ 泯14譌･莉･蜀・/ 閥7譌･莉･蜀・/ 笞ｫ譛滄剞蛻・ｌ
 */
export function getExpiryTier(expiryDate: string): ExpiryTier {
  const days = daysUntilExpiry(expiryDate);
  if (days < 0) return "expired";
  if (days <= 7) return "within7";
  if (days <= 14) return "within14";
  if (days <= 30) return "within30";
  return "safe";
}

export const EXPIRY_TIER_META: Record<
  ExpiryTier,
  { emoji: string; label: string; className: string }
> = {
  expired: { emoji: "笞ｫ", label: "譛滄剞蛻・ｌ", className: "bg-navy-dark text-white" },
  within7: { emoji: "閥", label: "7譌･莉･蜀・, className: "bg-danger text-white" },
  within14: { emoji: "泯", label: "14譌･莉･蜀・, className: "bg-[#eab308] text-navy-dark" },
  within30: { emoji: "泛", label: "30譌･莉･蜀・, className: "bg-warn text-white" },
  safe: { emoji: "泙", label: "31譌･莉･荳・, className: "bg-success text-white" },
};

--- filename: \src\lib\csv.ts ---

type Column<T> = { key: keyof T; label: string };

function escapeCsvCell(value: unknown): string {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return "";
  const str = String(value);
  if (/[",\n]/.test(str)) {
    return `"${str.replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
  }
  return str;
}

/**
 * CSV蜃ｺ蜉幢ｼ育ｬｬ16遶・啅TF-8蠖｢蠑擾ｼ峨・ * Excel縺ｧ縺ｮ譁・ｭ怜喧縺代ｒ驕ｿ縺代ｋ縺溘ａBOM繧剃ｻ倅ｸ弱☆繧具ｼ域律譛ｬ隱樣°逕ｨ縺ｧ荳闊ｬ逧・↑蟇ｾ遲厄ｼ峨・ */
export function toCsv<T extends Record<string, unknown>>(
  rows: T[],
  columns: Column<T>[]
): string {
  const header = columns.map((c) => escapeCsvCell(c.label)).join(",");
  const body = rows
    .map((row) => columns.map((c) => escapeCsvCell(row[c.key])).join(","))
    .join("\n");
  return "\uFEFF" + header + "\n" + body + "\n";
}

export function csvResponse(csv: string, filename: string): Response {
  const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(csv);
  return new Response(bytes, {
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "text/csv; charset=utf-8",
      "Content-Disposition": `attachment; filename="${filename}"`,
      "Content-Length": String(bytes.byteLength),
      "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff",
    },
  });
}



--- filename: \src\lib\date.ts ---

/** 譛邨よ擂蠎励°繧峨・邨碁℃譌･謨ｰ・育ｬｬ6遶縲梧怙邨よ擂蠎励°繧峨・譌･謨ｰ縲搾ｼ・*/
export function daysSince(isoDateString: string): number {
  const then = new Date(isoDateString).getTime();
  const now = Date.now();
  return Math.max(0, Math.floor((now - then) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)));
}

/** YYYY/MM/DD 陦ｨ遉ｺ */
/**
 * RC9菫ｮ豁｣: 縺薙ｌ縺ｾ縺ｧ d.getFullYear() / d.getHours() 遲峨・繝ｭ繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｫ繧ｿ繧､繝繧ｾ繝ｼ繝ｳ
 * getter繧剃ｽｿ縺｣縺ｦ縺・◆縺溘ａ縲√し繝ｼ繝舌・縺ｮ繧ｿ繧､繝繧ｾ繝ｼ繝ｳ險ｭ螳夲ｼ亥､壹￥縺ｮ蝣ｴ蜷・TC・峨↓
 * 萓晏ｭ倥＠縺ｦ譌･譛ｬ譎る俣縺ｨ繧ｺ繝ｬ縺ｦ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺輔ｌ縺ｦ縺・◆・域擂蠎怜ｱ･豁ｴ繝ｻ莠育ｴ・ｸ隕ｧ遲峨☆縺ｹ縺ｦ縺ｫ蠖ｱ髻ｿ・峨・ * 繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・縺ｮ螳溯｡檎腸蠅・↓髢｢繧上ｉ縺壼ｸｸ縺ｫ譌･譛ｬ譎る俣・・TC+9蝗ｺ螳夲ｼ峨〒陦ｨ遉ｺ縺吶ｋ縲・ */
export function formatDate(isoDateString: string | null | undefined): string {
  if (!isoDateString) return "-";
  // 譌･莉倥・縺ｿ・・YYY-MM-DD縲∽ｾ具ｼ壹・繝医Ν譛滄剞譌･・峨・繧ｿ繧､繝繧ｾ繝ｼ繝ｳ螟画鋤荳崎ｦ√・縺溘ａ縺昴・縺ｾ縺ｾ謨ｴ蠖｢縺吶ｋ
  if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(isoDateString)) {
    const [y, m, d] = isoDateString.split("-");
    return `${y}/${m}/${d}`;
  }
  return toJstDateString(isoDateString).replace(/-/g, "/");
}

/** YYYY/MM/DD HH:mm 陦ｨ遉ｺ・域擂蠎玲律譎ゅ↑縺ｩ繝ｻ譌･譛ｬ譎る俣蝗ｺ螳夲ｼ・*/
export function formatDateTime(isoDateString: string | null | undefined): string {
  if (!isoDateString) return "-";
  return `${formatDate(isoDateString)} ${toJstTimeString(isoDateString)}`;
}

/** <input type="datetime-local"> 逕ｨ縺ｮ蛟､・医Ο繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｫ繧ｿ繧､繝繧ｾ繝ｼ繝ｳ蝓ｺ貅厄ｼ・*/
export function toDateTimeLocalValue(date: Date): string {
  const pad = (n: number) => String(n).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${date.getFullYear()}-${pad(date.getMonth() + 1)}-${pad(date.getDate())}T${pad(
    date.getHours()
  )}:${pad(date.getMinutes())}`;
}

/**
 * RC8菫ｮ豁｣: DB縺ｮtimestamptz縺ｯUTC縺ｧ霑斐ｋ縺溘ａ縲∵枚蟄怜・繧貞腰邏斐↓slice(0,10)縺吶ｋ縺ｨ
 * 譌･譛ｬ譎る俣縺ｮ譌･莉倥→繧ｺ繝ｬ繧具ｼ域掠譛昴・譚･蠎励・莠育ｴ・′蜑肴律謇ｱ縺・↓縺ｪ繧狗ｭ会ｼ峨・ * 譌･譛ｬ譎る俣・・sia/Tokyo, UTC+9蝗ｺ螳夲ｼ峨ｒ蝓ｺ貅悶↓ YYYY-MM-DD / HH:mm 繧呈ｱゅａ繧九・ */
export function toJstDateString(isoString: string): string {
  const date = new Date(isoString);
  const jst = new Date(date.getTime() + 9 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  const pad = (n: number) => String(n).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${jst.getUTCFullYear()}-${pad(jst.getUTCMonth() + 1)}-${pad(jst.getUTCDate())}`;
}

export function toJstTimeString(isoString: string): string {
  const date = new Date(isoString);
  const jst = new Date(date.getTime() + 9 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  const pad = (n: number) => String(n).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${pad(jst.getUTCHours())}:${pad(jst.getUTCMinutes())}`;
}

/** 謖・ｮ壹＠縺滓律譛ｬ譎る俣縺ｮ譌･莉・YYYY-MM-DD)縺ｫ蟇ｾ蠢懊☆繧偽TC遽・峇縺ｮ髢句ｧ九・邨ゆｺ・SO譁・ｭ怜・繧定ｿ斐☆・・B繧ｯ繧ｨ繝ｪ逕ｨ・峨・*/
export function jstDateRangeToUtcIso(dateStr: string): { startIso: string; endIso: string } {
  // 譌･譛ｬ譎る俣 00:00:00 縺ｯ UTC-9譎る俣縲√▽縺ｾ繧雁燕譌･15:00 UTC
  const start = new Date(`${dateStr}T00:00:00+09:00`);
  const end = new Date(start.getTime() + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  return { startIso: start.toISOString(), endIso: end.toISOString() };
}

/**
 * RC9菫ｮ豁｣: <input type="datetime-local"> 縺ｮ蛟､・井ｾ・ "2026-07-27T16:58"・峨↓縺ｯ
 * 繧ｿ繧､繝繧ｾ繝ｼ繝ｳ諠・ｱ縺檎┌縺・◆繧√√◎縺ｮ縺ｾ縺ｾtimestamptz繧ｫ繝ｩ繝縺ｸ貂｡縺吶→Postgres蛛ｴ縺ｮ
 * 繧ｻ繝・す繝ｧ繝ｳ繧ｿ繧､繝繧ｾ繝ｼ繝ｳ・亥､壹￥縺ｮ蝣ｴ蜷・TC・峨〒隗｣驥医＆繧後※縺励∪縺・∵律譛ｬ譎る俣縺ｨ縺励※
 * 蜈･蜉帙＠縺滓凾蛻ｻ縺・譎る俣繧ｺ繝ｬ縺ｦ菫晏ｭ倥＆繧後ｋ・茨ｼ玖｡ｨ遉ｺ蛛ｴ縺ｧ譖ｴ縺ｫ+9譎る俣縺吶ｋ縺溘ａ莠碁㍾縺ｫ繧ｺ繝ｬ繧具ｼ峨・ * 縺薙％縺ｧ譏守､ｺ逧・↓ +09:00 繧剃ｻ倅ｸ弱＠縲∵ｭ｣縺励＞UTC迸ｬ髢薙↓螟画鋤縺励※縺九ｉ騾∽ｿ｡縺吶ｋ縲・ */
export function jstLocalToUtcIso(localDateTimeValue: string): string {
  // "YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm" 蠖｢蠑上ｒ諠ｳ螳壹らｧ偵′縺ゅｋ蝣ｴ蜷医ｂ縺昴・縺ｾ縺ｾ蛻ｩ逕ｨ縺吶ｋ縲・  const withOffset = `${localDateTimeValue}+09:00`;
  const date = new Date(withOffset);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) {
    // 諠ｳ螳壼､悶・蠖｢蠑上′譚･縺溷ｴ蜷医・迴ｾ蝨ｨ譎ょ綾縺ｫ繝輔か繝ｼ繝ｫ繝舌ャ繧ｯ縺吶ｋ・井ｿ晏ｭ倩・菴薙ｒ豁｢繧√↑縺・ｼ・    return new Date().toISOString();
  }
  return date.toISOString();
}

export function yen(n: number): string {
  return `ﾂ･${n.toLocaleString("ja-JP")}`;
}



--- filename: \src\lib\error-message.ts ---

/**
 * RC4菫ｮ豁｣: Supabase縺ｮ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺ｯJS縺ｮ Error 繧､繝ｳ繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繧ｹ縺ｧ縺ｯ縺ｪ縺上・ * { message, code, details, hint } 縺ｨ縺・≧蠖｢縺ｮ繝励Ξ繝ｼ繝ｳ繧ｪ繝悶ず繧ｧ繧ｯ繝茨ｼ・ostgrestError・峨・ * 縺薙ｌ縺ｾ縺ｧ蜷・園縺ｧ `e instanceof Error ? e.message : "豎守畑繝｡繝・そ繝ｼ繧ｸ"` 縺ｨ縺励※縺・◆縺溘ａ縲・ * Supabase縺ｮ譛ｬ蠖薙・繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ蜀・ｮｹ縺梧升繧翫▽縺ｶ縺輔ｌ縲∝ｸｸ縺ｫ豎守畑繝｡繝・そ繝ｼ繧ｸ縺縺代′陦ｨ遉ｺ縺輔ｌ縺ｦ縺・◆縲・ * 縺薙・髢｢謨ｰ縺ｯ縺ｩ縺｡繧峨・蠖｢縺ｮ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺梧擂縺ｦ繧よｭ｣縺励￥繝｡繝・そ繝ｼ繧ｸ繧貞叙繧雁・縺吶・ */
export function toErrorMessage(e: unknown, fallback: string): string {
  if (e instanceof Error) return e.message;
  if (e && typeof e === "object" && "message" in e && typeof (e as { message: unknown }).message === "string") {
    return (e as { message: string }).message;
  }
  if (typeof e === "string") return e;
  return fallback;
}

/**
 * RC7: Supabase/Postgrest縺ｮ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ繧ｪ繝悶ず繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医°繧・message繝ｻcode繝ｻdetails繝ｻhint 繧・ * 縺吶∋縺ｦ騾｣邨舌＠縺ｦ霑斐☆縲ゅ梧悽蠖薙・繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ蜀・ｮｹ繧定｡ｨ遉ｺ縺励※縺ｻ縺励＞縲阪→縺・≧隕∵悍縺ｫ蠢懊∴繧九◆繧√・ * 騾壼ｸｸ縺ｮ toErrorMessage() 繧医ｊ隧ｳ邏ｰ縺ｪ諠・ｱ繧貞・縺呻ｼ医・繝医Ν菫晏ｭ伜､ｱ謨玲凾縺ｮ隴ｦ蜻願｡ｨ遉ｺ遲峨↓菴ｿ逕ｨ・峨・ */
export function describeSupabaseError(e: unknown): string {
  if (!e || typeof e !== "object") return toErrorMessage(e, "隧ｳ邏ｰ荳肴・縺ｮ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ");

  const err = e as { message?: string; code?: string; details?: string; hint?: string };
  const parts: string[] = [];
  if (err.message) parts.push(err.message);
  if (err.code) parts.push(`code=${err.code}`);
  if (err.details) parts.push(`details=${err.details}`);
  if (err.hint) parts.push(`hint=${err.hint}`);
  return parts.length > 0 ? parts.join(" / ") : "隧ｳ邏ｰ荳肴・縺ｮ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ";
}



--- filename: \src\lib\pace.ts ---

import type { Customer } from "@/types/database";

export type PaceInfo = {
  label: string;
  avgIntervalDays: number | null;
  elapsedDays: number | null;
  /** 蟷ｳ蝮・擂蠎怜捉譛溘ｒ雜・∴縺ｦ譚･蠎励＠縺ｦ縺・↑縺・°・育ｬｬ25遶繝ｻ隨ｬ27遶縺ｮ騾夂衍蛻､螳壹↓菴ｿ逕ｨ・・*/
  isOverdue: boolean;
};

type PaceInput = Pick<Customer, "visit_count" | "first_visit_at" | "last_visit_at">;

/**
 * 譚･蠎励・繝ｼ繧ｹ蛻・梵・育ｬｬ27遶・峨・ * 蟷ｳ蝮・擂蠎鈴俣髫・= (譛邨よ擂蠎玲律 - 蛻晏屓譚･蠎玲律) / (譚･蠎怜屓謨ｰ - 1)
 * 譚･蠎怜屓謨ｰ縺・蝗樔ｻ･荳九・蝣ｴ蜷医・縲悟・譚･蠎励阪∵擂蠎怜ｱ･豁ｴ縺後↑縺・ｴ蜷医・縲・縲阪→縺吶ｋ縲・ */
export function computePace(customer: PaceInput): PaceInfo {
  if (!customer.first_visit_at || !customer.last_visit_at || customer.visit_count <= 0) {
    return { label: "-", avgIntervalDays: null, elapsedDays: null, isOverdue: false };
  }

  if (customer.visit_count === 1) {
    return { label: "蛻晄擂蠎・, avgIntervalDays: null, elapsedDays: 0, isOverdue: false };
  }

  const first = new Date(customer.first_visit_at).getTime();
  const last = new Date(customer.last_visit_at).getTime();
  const dayMs = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;

  const avgIntervalDays = Math.max(1, (last - first) / dayMs / (customer.visit_count - 1));
  const elapsedDays = Math.max(0, (Date.now() - last) / dayMs);

  let label: string;
  if (elapsedDays >= 180) {
    label = "蜊雁ｹｴ莉･荳頑擂蠎励↑縺・;
  } else if (elapsedDays >= 90) {
    label = "3縺区怦縺ｶ繧・;
  } else if (avgIntervalDays <= 8) {
    label = "豈朱ｱ";
  } else if (avgIntervalDays <= 16) {
    label = "譛・蝗・;
  } else if (avgIntervalDays <= 35) {
    label = "譛・蝗・;
  } else if (avgIntervalDays <= 70) {
    label = "2縺区怦縺ｫ1蝗・;
  } else {
    label = "荳榊ｮ壽悄";
  }

  // 蟷ｳ蝮・捉譛溘・1.5蛟阪ｒ雜・∴縺ｦ譚･蠎励′縺ｪ縺・ｴ蜷医ｒ縲悟捉譛溯ｶ・℃縲阪→縺吶ｋ
  const isOverdue = elapsedDays > avgIntervalDays * 1.5;

  return { label, avgIntervalDays, elapsedDays, isOverdue };
}

export type Database = {
  public: {
    Tables: {

      };
      tags: {

        Insert: Partial<Tag> & { name: string };
        Update: Partial<Tag>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      customer_tags: {
        Row: { customer_id: string; tag_id: string };
        Insert: { customer_id: string; tag_id: string };
        Update: { customer_id?: string; tag_id?: string };
        Relationships: [
          {
            foreignKeyName: "customer_tags_tag_id_fkey";
            columns: ["tag_id"];

          },

      };
      visits: {
        Row: Visit;

          primary_customer_id: string;

        };

        Relationships: [];
      };
      visit_members: {
        Row: VisitMember;
        Insert: Partial<VisitMember> & {
          visit_id: string;
          customer_id: string;
        };
        Update: Partial<VisitMember>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      bottles: {
        Row: Bottle;
        Insert: Partial<Bottle> & { customer_id: string; bottle_name: string };
        Update: Partial<Bottle>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      notes: {
        Row: Note;
        Insert: Partial<Note> & { customer_id: string; note: string };
        Update: Partial<Note>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      reservations: {
        Row: Reservation;
        Insert: Partial<Reservation> & {
          customer_id: string;
          reserved_at: string;
        };
        Update: Partial<Reservation>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      reservation_members: {
        Row: ReservationMember;
        Insert: Partial<ReservationMember> & {
          reservation_id: string;
          customer_id: string;
        };
        Update: Partial<ReservationMember>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      customer_views: {
        Row: { id: string; customer_id: string; viewed_by: string | null; viewed_at: string };
        Insert: { customer_id: string; viewed_by?: string | null };
        Update: { customer_id?: string; viewed_by?: string | null };
        Relationships: [];
      };
      audit_logs: {
        Row: AuditLog;
        Insert: Partial<AuditLog> & { action: string; table_name: string };
        Update: never;
        Relationships: [];
      };
      champagnes: {
        Row: Champagne;
        Insert: Partial<Champagne> & { customer_id: string; name: string };
        Update: Partial<Champagne>;
        Relationships: [];
      };
    };
    Views: {
      customer_month_stats: {
        Row: CustomerMonthStats;
        Relationships: [];
      };
    };
    Functions: {
      search_customers: {
        Args: { p_query: string };
        Returns: { customer_id: string }[];
      };
      create_visit_with_details: {
        Args: {
          p_customer_id: string | null;
          p_is_new_customer: boolean;
          p_new_customer_name: string | null;
          p_visited_at: string;
          p_people_count: number;
          p_companion_names: string[];
          p_amount: number;
          p_tip: number;
          p_payment_method: string;
          p_seat_type: string | null;
          p_receipt_required: boolean;
          p_receipt_name: string | null;
          p_memo: string | null;
          p_tag_ids: string[];
          p_reservation_id: string | null;
          p_new_customer_kana: string | null;
          p_companion_kanas: string[];
          p_new_customer_birthday: string | null;
          p_companion_birthdays: string[];
        };
        Returns: { visit_id: string; customer_id: string };
      };
      create_reservation_with_details: {
        Args: {
          p_customer_id: string | null;
          p_is_new_customer: boolean;
          p_new_customer_name: string | null;
          p_reserved_at: string;
          p_people_count: number;
          p_companion_names: string[];
          p_bottle_plan: boolean;
          p_tag_ids: string[];
          p_memo: string | null;
          p_new_customer_kana: string | null;
          p_companion_kanas: string[];
        };
        Returns: { reservation_id: string; customer_id: string };
      };
    };
  };
};

import { type NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { updateSession } from "@/lib/supabase/middleware";

/**
 * Next.js 16: middleware.ts 縺ｯ髱樊耳螂ｨ縺ｨ縺ｪ繧・proxy.ts 縺ｸ謾ｹ蜷阪＆繧後◆縲・ * 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ蜷阪・繧ｨ繧ｯ繧ｹ繝昴・繝磯未謨ｰ蜷阪ｒ "proxy" 縺ｫ螟画峩縺吶ｋ莉･螟悶√Ο繧ｸ繝・け縺ｯ螟画峩縺ｪ縺励・ * https://nextjs.org/docs/messages/middleware-to-proxy
 */
export async function proxy(request: NextRequest) {
  return await updateSession(request);
}

export const config = {
  matcher: [
    /*
     * 莉･荳九ｒ髯､縺丞・繝ｪ繧ｯ繧ｨ繧ｹ繝医↓繝槭ャ繝√☆繧・
     * - _next/static, _next/image (髱咏噪繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ)

     */
    "/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico|manifest.webmanifest|sw.js|offline.html|icons/).*)",
  ],

# Supabase 繧ｻ繝・ヨ繧｢繝・・謇矩・ｼ・inal迚茨ｼ・
## 1. 繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝井ｽ懈・
1. https://supabase.com 縺ｧ繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医ｒ譁ｰ隕丈ｽ懈・
2. Settings 竊・API 縺九ｉ莉･荳九ｒ繧ｳ繝斐・
   - Project URL 竊・`NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL`
     - 萓・ `https://xxxxx.supabase.co`・域忰蟆ｾ縺ｫ `/rest/v1` 繧剃ｻ倥￠縺ｪ縺・〒縺上□縺輔＞・・   - anon public key 竊・`NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`
3. 繧｢繝励Μ縺ｮ `.env.local` 縺ｫ雋ｼ繧贋ｻ倥￠・・.env.local.example` 繧貞盾辣ｧ・・
> URL縺ｫ `/rest/v1` 縺悟性縺ｾ繧後◆縺ｾ縺ｾ繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ縺励ｈ縺・→縺吶ｋ縺ｨ縲√Ο繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ逕ｻ髱｢縺ｫ
> 縲郡upabase URL縺ｮ譛ｫ蟆ｾ縺ｫ /rest/v1 縺悟性縺ｾ繧後※縺・∪縺吶阪→縺・≧蛻・°繧翫ｄ縺吶＞繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縺瑚｡ｨ遉ｺ縺輔ｌ縺ｾ縺呻ｼ・C2縺ｧ霑ｽ蜉・峨・
## 2. 繧ｹ繧ｭ繝ｼ繝樣←逕ｨ
Supabase繝繝・す繝･繝懊・繝峨・ SQL Editor 縺ｧ縲・*蠢・★縺薙・鬆・分**縺ｧ螳溯｡後＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・
1. `001_initial_schema.sql` 窶・繝・・繝悶Ν繝ｻ繧､繝ｳ繝・ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ繝ｻupdated_at繝医Μ繧ｬ繝ｼ繝ｻRLS譛牙柑蛹悶・莉ｮ繝昴Μ繧ｷ繝ｼ
2. `002_aggregates_and_rls.sql` 窶・髮・ｨ医き繝ｩ繝繝ｻ蜀崎ｨ育ｮ励ヨ繝ｪ繧ｬ繝ｼ繝ｻ讓ｩ髯仙挨RLS繝昴Μ繧ｷ繝ｼ縺ｸ縺ｮ鄂ｮ縺肴鋤縺・3. `003_search_and_views.sql` 窶・讀懃ｴ｢逕ｨ繧､繝ｳ繝・ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ・・g_trgm・峨・讓ｪ譁ｭ讀懃ｴ｢髢｢謨ｰ繝ｻ譛霑題ｦ九◆鬘ｧ螳｢繝・・繝悶Ν
4. `004_audit_log_triggers.sql` 窶・逶｣譟ｻ繝ｭ繧ｰ閾ｪ蜍戊ｨ倬鹸繝医Μ繧ｬ繝ｼ・・ustomers/visits/bottles/reservations/tags・・5. `005_bottle_quantity.sql` 窶・繝懊ヨ繝ｫ譛ｬ謨ｰ繧ｫ繝ｩ繝縺ｮ霑ｽ蜉・・C2・・6. `006_atomic_visit_and_reservation.sql` 窶・譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ繝ｻ莠育ｴ・匳骭ｲ縺ｮ繧｢繝医Α繝・け蛹悶√・繝医Ν遞ｮ鬘・繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ蛻･蜈･蜉帙∝・遖√・豕ｨ諢城｡ｧ螳｢繝輔Λ繧ｰ・・C4・・7. `007_rc5_fixes.sql` 窶・蜷御ｼｴ閠・・譚･蠎鈴寔險亥渚譏縲√Γ繝｢辟｡蜉ｹ蛹悶∵ｨｪ譁ｭ讀懃ｴ｢縺ｮ蟇ｾ雎｡諡｡螟ｧ縲√ち繧ｰ菴懈・繧偵せ繧ｿ繝・ヵ縺ｫ髢区叛縲∽ｸ隕ｧ縺ｮ螳牙ｮ壹た繝ｼ繝茨ｼ・C5・・8. `008_rc6_fixes.sql` 窶・縺九↑豁｣隕丞喧・医・繧峨′縺ｪ/繧ｫ繧ｿ繧ｫ繝頑ｨｪ譁ｭ讀懃ｴ｢・会ｼ・C6・・9. `009_rc7_fixes.sql` 窶・譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ繝ｻ莠育ｴ・匳骭ｲ縺ｧ縺ｮ譁ｰ隕城｡ｧ螳｢縺ｵ繧翫′縺ｪ蜈･蜉帙↓蟇ｾ蠢懶ｼ・C7・・10. `010_rc8_fixes.sql` 窶・譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ縺九ｉ繝懊ヨ繝ｫ繝ｻ繧ｷ繝｣繝ｳ繝代Φ蜃ｦ逅・ｒ蛻・屬縲∝酔莨ｴ閠・・縺ｵ繧翫′縺ｪ蟇ｾ蠢懶ｼ・C8繝ｻ譛驥崎ｦ・ｼ・11. `011_rc9_fixes.sql` 窶・bottles.quantity蛻励・蜀堺ｿ晁ｨｼ+繧ｹ繧ｭ繝ｼ繝槭く繝｣繝・す繝･蜀崎ｪｭ霎ｼ縲∝酔莨ｴ閠・莠ｺ譎ゅ・FOR繝ｫ繝ｼ繝嶺ｸ榊・蜷井ｿｮ豁｣縲∽ｺ育ｴ・・蜷御ｼｴ閠・・繧翫′縺ｪ縲√°縺ｪ讀懃ｴ｢縺ｮ蜀阪い繧ｵ繝ｼ繝茨ｼ・C9繝ｻ譛驥崎ｦ・ｼ・
CLI繧剃ｽｿ縺・ｴ蜷・

```

## 6. 驕主悉繝・・繧ｿ縺ｮ縺ｵ繧翫′縺ｪ譛ｪ險ｭ螳壹↓縺､縺・※

縺九↑讀懃ｴ｢・医・繧峨′縺ｪ/繧ｫ繧ｿ繧ｫ繝頑ｨｪ譁ｭ讀懃ｴ｢・峨・`customers.kana`・郁ｪｭ縺ｿ譁ｹ・峨′

`optional_find_customers_missing_kana.sql` 繧貞ｮ溯｡後☆繧九→縲∬ｪｭ縺ｿ譁ｹ縺梧悴險ｭ螳壹・鬘ｧ螳｢繧・譚･蠎怜屓謨ｰ縺ｮ螟壹＞鬆・↓荳隕ｧ縺ｧ縺阪∪縺吶ょｸｸ騾｣螳｢縺九ｉ蜆ｪ蜈育噪縺ｫ縲・｡ｧ螳｢邱ｨ髮・判髱｢

## 7. 譛ｬ逡ｪ髢句ｧ句燕縺ｮ繝・せ繝医ョ繝ｼ繧ｿ蜑企勁・磯㍾隕√・螳溯｡後・1蝗槭□縺托ｼ・

# both151'A CRM・域悽逡ｪ陦ｨ遉ｺ蜷搾ｼ壹″繧・▲縺ｦ縺・・・・

## 謚陦薙せ繧ｿ繝・け

- Next.js 16 (App Router, Turbopack) / React 19 / TypeScript
- Tailwind CSS v4

## 繝・ぅ繝ｬ繧ｯ繝医Μ讒区・

```
src/
  app/                       # 逕ｻ髱｢・・pp Router・・    login/                   # 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ

    visits/new/                # 譚･蠎礼匳骭ｲ
    customers/                  # 鬘ｧ螳｢荳隕ｧ繝ｻ譁ｰ隕冗匳骭ｲ繝ｻ隧ｳ邏ｰ繝ｻ邱ｨ髮・    search/                      # 鬘ｧ螳｢讀懃ｴ｢
    reservations/                 # 莠育ｴ・ｮ｡逅・    bottles/                       # 繝懊ヨ繝ｫ邂｡逅・    calendar/                       # 繧ｫ繝ｬ繝ｳ繝繝ｼ
    settings/                        # 險ｭ螳夲ｼ医ち繧ｰ繝ｻ繧ｹ繧ｿ繝・ヵ邂｡逅・・CSV蜃ｺ蜉帙・逶｣譟ｻ繝ｭ繧ｰ・・    api/export/                       # CSV蜃ｺ蜉妁PI繝ｫ繝ｼ繝・  components/
    layout/                    # Header / SideNav / BottomNav / AppShell / 繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ髢｢騾｣
    ui/                          # Button / Card / TextField
    customers/ visits/ reservations/ bottles/ calendar/ settings/ search/
  lib/
    supabase/                    # client.ts / server.ts / middleware.ts
    auth/                          # 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧､繝ｳ/繝ｭ繧ｰ繧｢繧ｦ繝医・迴ｾ蝨ｨ繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ蜿門ｾ・    data/                            # DB繧｢繧ｯ繧ｻ繧ｹ螻､・育判髱｢縺斐→縺ｮ繝・・繧ｿ蜿門ｾ鈴未謨ｰ・・    actions/                          # Server Actions・井ｿ晏ｭ倥・譖ｴ譁ｰ蜃ｦ逅・ｼ・    offline/                            # 繧ｪ繝輔Λ繧､繝ｳ繧ｭ繝･繝ｼ繝ｻ鬘ｧ螳｢讀懃ｴ｢繧ｭ繝｣繝・す繝･
    date.ts                              # 譌･莉倥・譌･譛ｬ譎る俣(JST)螟画鋤繝ｦ繝ｼ繝・ぅ繝ｪ繝・ぅ
    pace.ts bottle-expiry.ts bottle-types.ts error-message.ts csv.ts
  types/
    database.ts                          # Supabase蝙句ｮ夂ｾｩ
supabase/
  001縲・11_*.sql                          # 繝槭う繧ｰ繝ｬ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・井ｸ玖ｨ伜盾辣ｧ・・  README.md                               # Supabase繧ｻ繝・ヨ繧｢繝・・繝ｻ驕狗畑譁ｹ驥・  optional_find_customers_missing_kana.sql  # 莉ｻ諢上・遒ｺ隱咲畑繧ｹ繧ｯ繝ｪ繝励ヨ
```

## 繧ｻ繝・ヨ繧｢繝・・謇矩・ｼ医Ο繝ｼ繧ｫ繝ｫ髢狗匱・・
### 1. 萓晏ｭ倬未菫ゅ・繧､繝ｳ繧ｹ繝医・繝ｫ

```bash
npm install
```

### 2. 迺ｰ蠅・､画焚縺ｮ險ｭ螳・
```bash
cp .env.local.example .env.local
```

`.env.local` 縺ｫSupabase繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医・螳滄圀縺ｮURL繝ｻanon繧ｭ繝ｼ繧定ｨｭ螳壹＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞
・・.env.local.example` 縺ｫ蜿門ｾ玲婿豕輔ｒ險倩ｼ峨＠縺ｦ縺・∪縺呻ｼ峨・
### 3. Supabase繧ｹ繧ｭ繝ｼ繝槭・驕ｩ逕ｨ

`supabase/README.md` 縺ｮ謇矩・↓蠕薙＞縲～supabase/001_initial_schema.sql` 縺九ｉ
`supabase/011_rc9_fixes.sql` 縺ｾ縺ｧ縲・*逡ｪ蜿ｷ鬆・↓**SQL Editor縺ｧ螳溯｡後＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・
### 4. 譛蛻昴・邂｡逅・・い繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝井ｽ懈・

`supabase/README.md`縲・. 譛蛻昴・邂｡逅・・い繧ｫ繧ｦ繝ｳ繝井ｽ懈・縲阪ｒ蜿ら・縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲・
### 5. 髢狗匱繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・襍ｷ蜍・
```bash
npm run dev
```

http://localhost:3000 繧帝幕縺上→ `/login` 縺ｫ繝ｪ繝繧､繝ｬ繧ｯ繝医＆繧後∪縺吶・
### 6. 蜍穂ｽ懃｢ｺ隱咲畑繧ｳ繝槭Φ繝・
```bash
npx tsc --noEmit   # 蝙九メ繧ｧ繝・け
npx eslint .        # Lint
npm run build        # 譛ｬ逡ｪ繝薙Ν繝臥｢ｺ隱・```

## 譛ｬ逡ｪ蜈ｬ髢区焔鬆・
縺薙・繝ｪ繝昴ず繝医Μ縺ｯNext.js讓呎ｺ匁ｧ区・縺ｮ縺溘ａ縲〃ercel遲峨・Next.js蟇ｾ蠢懊・繧ｹ繝・ぅ繝ｳ繧ｰ縺ｫ縺昴・縺ｾ縺ｾ繝・・繝ｭ繧､縺ｧ縺阪∪縺吶・
1. **Supabase蛛ｴ縺ｮ貅門ｙ**
   - 譛ｬ逡ｪ逕ｨSupabase繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医ｒ菴懈・・磯幕逋ｺ逕ｨ縺ｨ蛻・￠繧九％縺ｨ繧呈耳螂ｨ・・   - `supabase/001`縲彖011`繧堤分蜿ｷ鬆・↓驕ｩ逕ｨ
